For the sake of the public interest, we urgently need to take appropriate measures, otherwise, the public will be disturbed and disputes will arise with the company, which may hinder local order. We are submitting another letter to your government for your review and approval, urgently requesting that you investigate and handle the previous case and order a stop to maintain public transportation. We await your orders."

The Development of the Sacred Heart Hospital 121

Adding a Radium Treatment Center, Maternity Hospital, and Outpatient Department

Its Various Facilities Can Be Called the Best in China

Shen Lu Bohong, Song Hancao, Le Zhenbao, Feng Bingnan, and others founded the Sacred Heart Hospital on Ningguo Road in Yangshupu. The hospital site covers more than 60 mu, and has four cement ward buildings, each of which can accommodate 150 people, divided into first, second, third, and fourth class, with both men and women admitted. Since its opening ten years ago, it has achieved remarkable results. All patients who have sought treatment have expressed satisfaction with the medical treatment and nursing care. In addition to treating nearby poor people who have suffered falls, cuts, burns, etc., without charge, free clinics are held every afternoon, reaching 500 to 600 people. Recently, under the careful planning of Hospital Director Lu Bohong, Hospital Affairs Director Lu Yingeng, and Medical Director Song Wusheng, the hospital has made even greater progress. A radium treatment center has recently been added, and all radium treatment equipment has been purchased, worth more than 200,000 yuan, specializing in the treatment of gastric cancer, scrofula, and other difficult and complicated diseases such as internal and external tumors, all of which have immediate and miraculous effects. This is a newly invented medical weapon, and it is still the only one in China. There are also two large and small X-ray machines with extremely strong therapeutic power. At the same time, Director Lu, in view of the fact that there is still a lack of maternity hospitals in the eastern part of Shanghai, and in response to the requests of local people, has specially added a maternity hospital, hiring obstetrician gynecologists to be responsible for delivery, and purchasing a number of sanitary vehicles for patients to use at any time. For the sake of general benefit, it has been decided that, starting from March 1, an outpatient department will be established for internal and external medicine and other departments. The doctors who will take turns in charge of diagnosis and treatment, such as Medical Director Shi Deli, Song Wusheng, internal and external medicine doctors Pan Weicen, Shi Demin, radium X-ray director Ge Chengzhi, Zhang Youmei, specially invited doctors Xie Bi, the Boro siblings, Mude, Bumei, Engel, Xie Yingrui, Huang Fei, Liu Zunzhi, Chen Bangyu, etc., are all leaders in the Chinese and Western medical circles in Shanghai.

The company immediately reported to the competent official department, and party and government agencies all sent personnel to investigate and announced the cause of the accident. The details are recorded as follows.

Workers Burned to Death 122

After the firefighters managed to dig out the workers who were burned to death, there were a total of seventeen, including two male workers and fifteen female workers. According to their work numbers, names, native places, ages, and families, they are as follows: 1. No. 469, Zhang Fucai, 23 years old, Nanxiang, family member Zhang Haijiang; 2. Body Examination and Collection 123

Yesterday, the Jiangyin Guild Hall prepared seventeen coffins and separately collected the workers who were burned to death, with five pieces of silk burial clothing and one quilt each, temporarily placing them on the open space in the factory, waiting for the court to examine them before putting them into coffins. At 4:00 p.m., the local court dispatched Prosecutor Ouyang Tao to rush to examine the bodies separately, and then the Jiangyin Guild Hall collected them, and the bereaved families received them. As for those who have not been claimed, they will be temporarily housed by the Jiangyin Guild Hall at Pushan Villa for claim. At the same time, the company set up a reception center for the bereaved families yesterday and received representatives of each family to discuss the solution. The affected workers will probably be compensated 600 yuan each according to the Factory Law, and a memorial service for the deceased workers will be held regularly in the No. 1 factory. The circumstances of the incident will be reported to the Social Bureau.

Company Report 124

The Yonghe Industrial Company submitted a report to the Social Bureau yesterday, stating, "Regarding the matter of reporting the cause of the factory fire, please review and approve: Our company has a factory located at the end of Xibaoxing Road and Minsheng Road in Zhabei, manufacturing cosmetics and rubber products. During the January 28th Incident last year, the front part of the factory was destroyed by artillery fire. In order to maintain the livelihood of the workers, we immediately repaired and started work in the remaining bungalows. Unexpectedly, at about 11:00 a.m. on the 27th of this month, a fire suddenly broke out in the rubber department's drying room. Before we could notice, the steam cylinder in the drying room had become heated and exploded, causing the house to collapse. A small number of workers who did not have time to escape were tragically affected. All the injured have been sent to the hospital for treatment. Our company's factory equipment has been investigated and recorded by your bureau, but we did not expect the disaster to come unexpectedly. Our company has suffered greatly from the destruction of the violent Japanese, and we have been operating painstakingly, but we have not even restored one-tenth. Unexpectedly, we have encountered another accident, and we are particularly saddened by the affected workers. We are now trying to handle the aftermath and compensation. All the circumstances of the fire are hereby reported. Please review and record."

Party and Government Investigation 125

Yesterday at 10:00 AM, the Social Affairs Bureau dispatched Tian Heqing, director of the factory inspection division, and Li Chong, et al., to conduct an investigation for verification. Also yesterday at 11:00 AM, the Municipal Party Headquarters sent Zhao Erchang, an officer from the civil training section, to investigate the truth. Afterward, Director Tian of the Social Affairs Bureau discussed the incident, saying that after the factory disaster occurred, the bureau immediately dispatched factory inspectors Li Chongpu and others to investigate. According to reports, the cause of the accident was similar to that of the Zhengtai Factory, also due to the burning of "xi silin" (likely a phonetic transliteration of "xylene") in the coating room. The air temperature in the steam room, which adjoined the coating room, and the air pressure inside the cylinder suddenly increased several times, causing it to explode. There were originally seventeen workers in the coating room, three of whom died instantly because they could not escape. The canvas shoe factory on the side of the steam cylinder room collapsed due to the strong vibration of the steam cylinder, crushing fourteen female workers to death and injuring more than twenty. Yesterday, one male worker died in the hospital due to severe injuries. Apart from ten who were hospitalized, the other slightly injured workers have all been discharged. It was found that the factory's equipment had been inspected by the bureau's factory inspectors on November 17th. At that time, the canvas shoe section had not yet started work, but the safety equipment on the steam cylinder was relatively complete, and the inspectors strictly instructed the factory to handle it properly to prevent explosions. This steam cylinder explosion was not due to the poor safety equipment of the steam cylinder itself, but because the temperature around the outside of the steam cylinder suddenly increased, and the air pressure inside the steam cylinder increased accordingly, leading to the explosion, which was very unfortunate. For the sake of convenience, rubber factories in the city often combine coating and steaming work in one room, which makes it easy for the xylene used in coating to catch fire and cause the steam cylinder to explode. To avoid similar disasters, the coating room and the steam cylinder room should be completely separated, and workshops should not be set up on the upper floor of the steam cylinder room. Fortunately, the steam cylinder room of the Yongru Factory was a single-story building, otherwise, this tragedy would have been even more serious than the Zhengtai Factory incident. However, in order to reduce the chance of fire in the xylene used in the coating room, the design of the coating oil drums urgently needs to be improved. The bureau has drafted measures to improve the safety problems of rubber factories in the city and will order all factories to comply with them.

Huang Baohua Released from Kidnapping 126

Held in Bandit Den for Two Weeks

Huang Baohua, an accountant at the Ruikang Pigment Company on Shandong Road in the Shanghai International Settlement, was kidnapped by bandits at the intersection of Avenue Edward VII and Rue Grollier in the French Concession on the evening of the 12th of this month. It is now heard that Huang returned home safely from the bandit den yesterday morning at about 5:00 AM. In total, he was kidnapped for more than two weeks. Huang is a native of Jiangyin, 50 years old, and has worked as an accountant at Ruikang for many years. He lives at No. 25 Rue Grollier in the French Concession. At about 7:00 PM on the evening of the 12th of this month, Huang returned from a spring banquet at a friend's house. While riding in a chartered car through the intersection of Avenue Edward VII and Rue Grollier, he was suddenly dragged down by three or four bandits and forced into a car that had been parked on the side of the road, and driven away. Only this morning was he able to escape.

Dock Coolies Brawl, Causing Trouble 127

Gao Zuoqiao Dies Tragically

There is a gang of "wild chicken" coolies on the Pudong Company's dock, all from Hubei province. In addition to working as laborers, they also make a living by smuggling "swept-package" goods (i.e., goods that evade taxes). Yesterday afternoon, Gao Zuoqiao and his gang appropriated some smuggled goods, and did not share the profits, which was questioned by Chen Guiqing and others on the opposing side. A conflict ensued, resulting in a brawl resembling a械斗 (xie dou, a large-scale clan fight). Gao Zuoqiao was the target of the crowd, and suffered injuries all over his body, immediately falling unconscious. The Third District Police Department dispatched police officers to arrest Chen Guiqing, Ji Jinkui, Wang Daosheng, Wu Luhou, Liu Ali, and others. The injured person was carried to the Baolong Hospital for treatment by his elder brother, Gao Zuoying. However, due to the severity of his injuries, he died this morning. The Third District Police Department was immediately notified and the defendants were transferred to the local court. At the same time, the local bailiff was ordered to report to the court for an autopsy.

Russian Woman Found to Have Died from Miscarriage and Peritonitis 128

The Russian woman, Akos Danuo, also known as Anasia Danxue Yin Nuo Kai Dinaxie Ke Ning, residing at No. 47 Tangshan Road, died from a miscarriage at Hongen Hospital on the 24th of this month. The body was sent to the Feilun Autopsy Institute by the Huishan Patrol Room, where the First Special District Local Court appointed Prosecutor Guo Wei, along with forensic doctor Wei Ligong, clerk Wang Zuyi, and others, to inspect the body and order a rescheduled autopsy. This information has already been recorded in this newspaper. Forensic Doctor Wei of the First Special Court, along with doctors from the Public Works Department, dissected the body, and the result was that the deceased died from miscarriage and peritonitis. Yesterday morning, the period for re-examination arrived again, and Prosecutor Guo and forensic doctors arrived at the autopsy institute again. According to the report of the Western Detective Meng Aisi, according to the report of the doctor Huotuoliede (likely a phonetic transliteration) of the Public Charity Hospital, the deceased went to the hospital on the fourth day with internal bleeding, and was discharged on the eleventh day. On the fifteenth, I went to her home, and the next day, the deceased went to the hospital again and suddenly had a miscarriage. At that time, only the nurse was there, and the placenta had not been delivered and the bleeding did not stop. The next day, I took her bag down, causing my finger to rupture the woman's blood vessels. On the fourth day after delivery, she developed peritonitis. The deceased's poison gas did not spread, and her life could still be saved. Surgery was also feared to cause death. The Russian midwife Boerhuotuo (likely a phonetic transliteration) also testified that she was 42 years old, residing at No. 19, Lane 166, Mao Hai Road. I no longer work in this profession and have relied on my husband for more than two years. I did not perform an abortion for the deceased. On December 15 last year, the deceased came to ask if I could perform an abortion, and I immediately refused to see her. The report was obtained, and it was concluded that the deceased Russian woman Akos Danuo died from a miscarriage and peritonitis. The body was handed over to the Health Department of the Public Works Department for coffin preparation.

Formal Union of Husband and Wife, Mother-in-Law Sues for Abduction and Escape 129

Hu Xu Has Other Intentions

Hu Lianyuan Has a Clear Conscience

Hu Xu, a native of Ningbo residing at No. 400, Rixin Lane, Tangshan Road, previously hired a lawyer in the First Special District Court to accuse Hu Lianyuan, an employee of the Weiren Foreign Company, of abducting her 18-year-old daughter, Hu Lingzhen, and filed a civil suit, requesting the court to order the defendant to pay alimony of 20,000 yuan in one lump sum. The Special Court had summoned him once, but because the accuser did not arrive, it was adjourned to a later date. It is now learned that the defendant, Hu Lianyuan, has also hired lawyer Aiyafu to submit a statement and file a countersuit for false accusation. The original statement vaguely stated that the defendant was formally engaged to Ms. Du Lingzhen on the tenth day of the eighth month of the lunar calendar last year through the introduction of Hu Dingjia and Ke Niangniang, and with the consent of both parents. (Lingzhen was originally surnamed Du, her biological father died early, and her mother remarried, so Hu Benwei, so her surname is Hu.) At that time, the matchmaker sent a betrothal gift of 220 yuan. On the fourteenth day of the eleventh month of the year, both parents invited Pastor Yu Zhizhai to officiate the wedding at Jinglin Church on Kunshan Road. In the evening, a banquet was held at the Dazhonghua Restaurant, and female relatives such as Lu Shun'e and Ma Rumei also attended the wedding banquet. However, the day before the wedding, the plaintiff wanted to extort a gift of 100 yuan, but the defendant only gave 50 yuan, which did not meet her wishes, and she held a grudge in her heart. She refused to sign the marriage certificate, but was later reconciled. On the thirteenth of this month, the plaintiff reported to the Huishan Patrol Room that the defendant had abducted her daughter, hoping to take advantage of the defendant. Because the defendant had nothing to hide, he went to the patrol room with Lingzhen to confront her. After investigation by the patrol room, it was determined that the defendant and Lingzhen were indeed formally married and there was no abduction. The plaintiff was reprimanded, but the plaintiff became angry and entrusted a lawyer to file a lawsuit. It was found that all the allegations made by the plaintiff were false. It was also found that the plaintiff made false accusations intending to subject others to criminal punishment, which constitutes the crime of false accusation under Article 180 of the Criminal Code. It should be declared that the defendant is innocent and the plaintiff should be punished for false accusation. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Wu Zehan opened the Eighth Criminal Court to summon the defendant and Hu Lingzhen. Ms. Hu was fair-skinned, petite and exquisite, wearing a printed cheongsam, a short coat, silk stockings and leather shoes, and her hair was loose. She sat in the audience, calm and smiling from time to time. The plaintiff, Hu Xu, claimed to be 38 years old. I married at the age of 19, and my husband died the following May. In August, I remarried Hu Benwei. Lingzhen was born to my previous husband. She studied and grew up in Fengtian. Unexpectedly, Lingzhen ran away on November 8 last year, and I later learned that she was abducted by the defendant, so I filed a lawsuit. Questioning the defendant, he confessed that Hu Dingjia and Liu Niangniang acted as matchmakers to the plaintiff and paid a gift of 220 yuan. Later, they formally married at Jinglin Church and invited Yu Zhizhai to officiate the wedding. He presented the red wedding certificate to the court. The rest of his confession was the same as his statement, omitted. According to Hu Lingzhen, she agreed to marry Hu Lianyuan this time with her mother's consent, and the matchmaker brought a gift of 220 yuan. Judge Wu verified the confessions and declared to the plaintiff that according to modern criminal law, as long as men and women are over 16 years old, agree to each other, and have the introduction of two or more people, it becomes effective. The consent of the parents is not a problem. Now that the defendant has submitted a formal marriage certificate, it is naturally considered legal. Therefore, before the start of the debate, he can withdraw the case and file a lawsuit in the civil court. However, the plaintiff stubbornly refused to understand, so the lawyer debated to the end. Judge Wu ruled Hu Lianyuan not guilty.

Record of Trial of Murder and Robbery 130

Jin Jiulin, supervisor of the special agency of the French Patrol Room, detective Hong Ziying, private detective Qin Youyu, and others, arrested five bandits in Room 340 of the Asia Hotel, No. 340 Avenue Edward VII, at 5:00 AM on the 15th of last month: Hua Yunlong (also known as the coolie A Mao), Lu Hongquan, Wang Ruijin, Lu Quangen, and Shi A'gen. They seized a pistol and six bullets, and found out that the bandits had robbed the home of Jin Xiaofan, a native of Anhui, at No. 1 Yiheli, Beile Road, on the night of January 3, shooting and killing the victim. They were sent to the Second Special District Court to file a public prosecution, interrogate, and investigate, as reported in previous newspapers. The detectives have now found that the bandits first colluded with Zhang Hongshan, Yang Yonglin, and others who are at large to rob Zhang Qinzhou, a bill collector of the French Electric Light Company at No. 325 Annakin Road, Xu Ansheng's meat shop at No. 72 Bair Road, and Xu Wanmin's home at No. 11 Xinkangli, Mafang Street, and have recorded their confessions. Yesterday, they were sent to the court again. In the afternoon, Judge Xiong Huiping presided over the trial in the First Criminal Court. First, lawyer Gu Shouxi of the Patrol Room stated the Patrol Room's investigation situation, and the victim's widow, Jin Wangshi, recounted the situation of her husband Jin Xiaofan's murder, requesting a thorough investigation to avenge her husband's death. Then, the victims recounted the process of being robbed. Hua Yunlong confessed that Zhang Hongshan, who was at large, had the idea, and colluded with the people on trial and Yang Yonglin, who was at large, to rob Jin Xiaofan's home. I was watching the wind outside the door and shared the loot. Lu Zhang and others went inside to rob and shot the victim. The four robbers Wang, Lu, and Shi also confessed to robbing the homes of the victims together and jointly hired lawyer Zhu Yonglie for defense. The court ordered a rescheduled trial. The defendants were returned to custody.

Woman Dies Tragically from Coal Poisoning 131

The abandoned small steamer "New Sielge" is docked on the Huangpu River at Guangxing Wharf. Liu Zhisheng, a native of Ningbo, was hired to watch the boat. Liu lived there with his family, including Liu's wife, Liu Luo, 34 years old, a six-year-old daughter, and his son Chengcai, who was just nine months old. Because they lived and ate there, there was always a coal stove in the cabin. The day before yesterday afternoon, Liu Luo bought a few fish, slaughtered and ate them, and went to sleep with her two children. Liu himself had other work to do. When he returned home at dawn, he found his wife and two children lying stiff in the cabin. The charcoal fire in the stove had not gone out. He quickly dragged them out to the dock. The girl was rescued and woke up, but his wife and others were already dead. He immediately reported to the Water Patrol Room, and Detective Qu and two doctors went inside to investigate. The room was full of foul gas, which made people nauseous. It was impossible to determine whether the deceased died from coal poisoning or from poisoning from the fish they had eaten. The detective was ordered to take the corpses to the South Wharf for resuscitation and report to the local court, which appointed Prosecutor Ouyang and others to inspect the scene. They confirmed that the corpses had died from coal poisoning and ordered the family to collect them for burial.

Assassination on Milu Road 132

Yin A'xiang Remarried Twice After Becoming a Widow

Small Ruffian Jealous of Adultery, Opens Fire and Kills Coppersmith

At about 7:00 AM yesterday morning, an assassination occurred at the entrance of Xinle Lane, Milu Road, Nanyang Bridge, French Concession. The victim was a coppersmith, who died immediately. The murderer was a hooligan who escaped on the spot. The motive for the murder was a love rivalry. Details are recorded below:

Widow Remarries 133

There is a woman surnamed Yin from Shaoxing, named A'xiang, who is now 25 years old. At the age of 17, she was married to Wang Yongzhao, a farmer from the same village, by her parents. Not long after, Wang suddenly died of illness, leaving behind a son named Zhigang. Ms. Yin became a widow at a young age, and her parents' family was poor. She had no choice but to bring her young son to Shanghai to seek refuge with relatives and make a living. However, after arriving in Shanghai, she was alone and unable to make a living. Later, a person surnamed Chen acted as a matchmaker, and she remarried to Wang Xitang, also from the same village. Wang is 36 years old this year, has no occupation, and is actually a rogue hooligan.

Encountering the Wrong Person 134

After Yin married Wang, she did not expect Wang to be a libertine. As time went by, she realized that she had been deceived, but she only resigned herself to her fate and cried secretly. Unexpectedly, in less than a year, Wang treated her like old shoes, adding "xiachu" (likely a reference to physical punishment). Wang had an old father named Wang Wenkui, who never approved of what Xitang had done. Ms. Yin often complained to Wang's father, asking for help.

Remarriage Midway 135

Wang Wenkui, knowing that Xitang of the Zhi Xitang family was inherently violent, strongly advised Ms. Yin to find a way to divorce him. At the time, Xitang actually demanded a price of one thousand yuan, which was eventually reduced to four hundred yuan. Both parties agreed that the man and woman were free to marry and remarry as they pleased. This took place in the late tenth lunar month of last year. After the two parties severed ties, Ms. Yin soon became acquainted with a coppersmith named Peng Quanbao. Peng was twenty-four years old, originally from the Lvsi area, and currently worked at Yongtai Metal Casting Factory on Six Ma Road, living together with Ms. Yin.

After Ms. Yin and Peng became intimate, she, along with her eight-year-old son Zhigang, rented Room 6 in Xinle Lane, Nanyang Bridge, French Concession, on the upper floor, western middle room, of Yao Yongji Electroplating Factory (rent of nine yuan per month) to live together. Peng's second elder brother, Miaoqi, worked as a foreman at Yao Yongji, and his eldest brother, Miaolin, was currently an employee at a certain metal workshop at Hongqiao Tou in the Nanshi district, having returned to his hometown on business a few days ago. Unexpectedly, yesterday morning at 7:15 AM, Peng got up and went to the tiger stove at the Milu Road intersection to get hot water. Just as he reached the alley entrance, Ms. Yin's ex-husband, Wang Xitang, who had been lying in wait, saw Peng and immediately drew a pistol, aiming at Peng's head and firing two shots. One bullet hit the left temple, and the other hit the upper lip. Peng immediately fell to the ground, blood gushing like a fountain. At the same time, Yao Yongji's colleagues, hearing the alarm, rushed out, but the assailant had already fled without a trace. Peng died from his serious injuries.

Ms. Yin immediately reported to the police station. The police chief sent detectives to investigate. They first rushed Quanbao to Renji Hospital, but because the injuries were to vital areas, he died shortly after arriving at the hospital. The hospital notified the police station, and the Tongren Fuyuan branch ordered undertakers to carry the body for examination and report to the Second Special District Court for inspection. The police are now strictly investigating the assailant and will punish him according to the law.

Liu Fugao also died that evening from his injuries. The bodies of both were examined yesterday (i.e., the 16th) at the Tongren Fuyuan Hall by a prosecutor from the Second Special District Court. Zhu Guting was shot in the chest and back, and Liu Fugao was shot through the abdomen. The two unidentified individuals were wounded in their hands and feet and were treated at the hospital. The incident was reported as such.

The cross-border police interfered with two women riding in a car and, seeing a large crowd of onlookers, arbitrarily fired shots to disperse the crowd, firing several shots and killing and wounding many people. This is an abuse of power, a deliberate killing. If this case is not severely punished, citizens will be in danger at any time and in any place. We urgently request the relevant departments to negotiate swiftly with the French Concession authorities, ensuring that the culprit is punished according to the law, that the deceased's family is generously compensated, and that guarantees are made that such incidents will not occur again. We pray that human life will be valued and security will be guaranteed.

Expansion of the Second Special District Court

The Second Special District Court of the French Concession has recently experienced a large increase in civil and criminal cases. The original six courtrooms are insufficient, and the office space at 4 Hozhi Lane across the street is too small. Therefore, the court has requested the French Municipal Council to lease the council's three-story Western-style building at 16 Xuehuali Road (i.e., the residence of the former head of the Western Prison, next door to the court along the road). After the council approved, the court hired craftsmen to renovate the building. Once completed, two courtrooms will be set up downstairs, and the prosecutor's office and judicial police office will be moved to the second floor. The third floor will still be used by the Municipal Council as an office for the judicial advisor, moving the judicial advisor's office and the police lawyer's office currently located inside the Municipal Council at Dazimingzhong to that location for convenience. Furthermore, the current French Municipal Council judicial advisor, Mr. Duna (translator), has returned to his country for vacation and relinquished his position, to be replaced by Mr. Jadang (translator, former assistant judge of the French Court), who has returned to Shanghai from his home country.

Planning for Pudong Water Plant

The Municipal Public Utilities Bureau Plans to Find Other Ways

The Municipal Public Utilities Bureau has long planned to develop the Pudong area and build a water plant. The site for the plant has also been selected. The reason for the delay is due to the municipal government's financial difficulties. According to the Municipal Public Utilities Bureau, they originally planned to start construction by the end of last year, but due to the weakened post-war economy, municipal revenue has decreased, while expenditures have increased. As a result, the plan could not be realized. Moreover, the current price of gold has risen sharply, and the cost of purchasing machinery has greatly increased compared to the original budget. According to recent statistics, it would cost no less than 300,000 yuan to start construction. However, the development of the Pudong area cannot be delayed. Therefore, it has been decided to find other ways to start construction as soon as possible.

Wang Jingchu Committed Suicide

Wang Jingchu, an old clerk from Pudong, aged fifty-nine, at Dachang Silk Store, No. 3 Mingguo Road, Xiaodongmen, had worked in the store for a long time. Wang was frugal and had no vices. Woman from Yutan Accuses Aunt and Younger Uncle of Defamation

The woman Yao Xiuying, whose husband Gao Jinzhang used to run a fish stall at the Xiakou vegetable market, had saved some money and had a seven-year-old son. Last year, Gao suddenly fell ill and died. Yao Xiuying continued to run the fish stall. Yao Xiuying's aunt, Gao Liu, and younger uncle, Gao Arui, coveted Yao's fish stall and savings and repeatedly forced her to remarry and tried to drive her out. They used various methods to falsely accuse Yao of misconduct. Feeling wronged by this insult, she hired lawyer Yang Ruinian to file a lawsuit in the First Special District Court against Gao Liu and Gao Arui for defamation, requesting that they be punished according to the criminal law for harming her reputation. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Liu Yugui of the Special District Court opened the court to summon the defendants. According to Gao Yao, since her husband's death, even before the mourning period of two sevens (fourteen days) was over, her aunt and uncle abused her, intending to drive her out of the house and forcing her to remarry, and falsely accusing her of having a lover and renting a small house to serve as grounds for driving her out. The neighbors are aware of this matter, but they are afraid of the defendants' violence and dare not testify in court. The two defendants denied the aforementioned allegations. The court then ordered the commencement of arguments, and after lawyer Yang's arguments, Judge Liu ordered that a date be set for sentencing.

Buddhist Bookstore Spreads Dharma Sound 137

This city's Buddhist Bookstore, in order to promote Buddhism, has decided that starting March 1st, Dharma questions and answers will be broadcast every morning by the editor, Dharma Master Huizhou, and layman Shi Wuwei, a clerk, via the Yongsheng Wireless Radio Station on Nanjing Road. They will also respectfully recite the entire Diamond Sutra to pray for the nation and alleviate disasters. Ladies and gentlemen from all walks of life who have wireless radios at home and have questions about Buddhism can write to the bookstore or the Yongsheng Wireless Radio Station. The bookstore will answer the questions through broadcasts every morning.

Fire on Caishi Road

Yesterday at 3:36 PM, a fire broke out suddenly in the dormitory above the Yuanchangsheng Candle Shop at No. 63-65 Caishi Road in the French Concession. The owner of the shop is Sheng Xingshou. Smoke immediately filled the air, and the fire blazed fiercely, spreading to two rooms on the upper floor. The fire brigade rushed to the scene with pumps and put out the fire with great effort.

Miscellaneous News

Copper Coins Plunge, Peddlers Suffer: The exchange rate between silver dollars and copper coins in this city has continued to rise in recent days. Yesterday, the exchange rate displayed at various small money changers and cigarette paper shops exceeded 3,000 cash coins per silver dollar. A small silver coin (double dime) could be exchanged for six dimes, which is twelve jiao, plus five copper coins. Corner scrap was exchanged for 490 cash coins. With such a large increase in the exchange rate, peddlers are crying out in distress.

City News

Zhanghua and Others Jointly Establish Retail Department: Zhanghua Woolen Textile Factory, National Porcelain Enamelware Business Office, and Zhonghua Industrial Factory in this city are all the largest domestic goods factories in China. It is reported that starting March 4th, they will establish a joint retail department in the Penglai City Market in the Nanshi area, selling high-quality products from each factory, such as Zhanghua's various woolen fabrics, broadcloth, camel hair, woolen yarn, etc., Zhonghua's various silks, satin, mohair, scarves, lace, etc., and domestic enamelware such as basins, pots, and porcelain ware. Everything is available, and in order to promote domestic goods, the prices are especially discounted.

Gu Tianren Holds Installment Discount Sale: Gu Tianren Ginseng, Bird's Nest, and Chinese Medicine Store on Shandong Road in this city has been operating successfully since its reorganization last year. It is now reported that the store is holding an installment discount sale to benefit customers. Discounts will be given every solar calendar 1st and 15th, and lunar calendar new moon and full moon, with exceptions, plus one day discount every Sunday. Decoction pieces and pills are sold at 80% or 90% of the original price. Rejuvenating Ginseng Pills, regardless of size, buy two get one free. Ginseng and bird's nest products are sold at 90% of the original price. This is the most unique feature in the discounted sales.

Recent News from the China National Goods Company: Since the opening grand discount of the China National Goods Company (Nanjing Road) in the Mainland Commercial Center on February 9th, the term is about to expire. The special-priced products sold daily are all selected high-quality goods, and the prices are the lowest in Shanghai. It is reported that the discount opportunity is only available for one day today. The company's securities department, located in the store, sells a lot every day. In addition to purchasing various domestic goods, they can also be exchanged for cash at the New China Trust and Savings Bank, setting a new record for gift certificates.

The Further Adventures of Hawthorne: All those who love to read detective novels must know the outstanding private detective of his time, Hawthorne. It is truly a good reading material in the recent publishing world.　　The China Monthly: The China Monthly, compiled by the China Daily, is published today. The style is similar to the New York Times Magazine in the United States and Asahi Weekly in the Asahi Shimbun of Japan, and the binding is exquisite and lovely. As for the novelty of the content and the completeness of the collection, although we dare not determine that it can release a ray of dawn on the lonely literary world of our country, there is no doubt that it will give a huge impulse. Reader Consultant

Sports and Public Health Issues (Continued) 142

Letter from Mr. Xu Xianfu of this city

Above, we have already raised many issues for discussion, which is enough to prove the danger and unsuitability of modern sports in China. Finally, let us solve the question of whether sports (as a whole) can be the way out for China? Of course, the discussion of this question must involve what is China's true way out? Let's first look at where the crux of China's illness lies? Is it ignorance, poverty, or weakness?

Initially, discussing weakness, we must ask why the Chinese people know that they are weak, and where is that seen? Is it the emigration rate? Or disease statistics? Needless to say, China lacks precise statistics. Even with current statistics, if the mortality rate is indeed very high, does this mortality rate exclude the causes of war, natural disasters, killings, and plagues? Do the disease statistics consist of substantial data, or do they exclude plagues? Before I have sufficient evidence regarding the issue of the weakness of the Chinese people to persuade me to advocate it, I cannot blindly follow the general promotion of sports to save weakness. (See previous remarks for further discussion). Some people say that Japan's strength lies in the prevalence of sports, but they do not know that such a statement is as absurd as Montesquieu's inference that the British political system is based on the separation of powers. We know that Japan's strength, although not absolute, is mostly due to the fact that peddlers, young people, and children are constantly reading. I remember Mr. Wang Yunwu once told us that in a Japanese inn, he saw the child who opened the door still reading a book while opening the door, and what he was reading was not a novel but a series of knowledge books and history and geography. These may be digressions, please forgive me. Next, discussing poverty, why is China poor? Positively, we cannot control nature, that is, we cannot utilize nature, and we lack productivity, so the country has little wealth. Negatively, we cannot control society, such as political failures and social disorders, which destroy productivity, and the country's wealth decreases. Therefore, to alleviate poverty, we must first be able to control nature and control society, and the implementation of these two methods is entirely related to the level of national knowledge. In the final analysis, China's way out lies in saving ignorance.

Finally, how do we save ignorance? Fascism is based on the idea of the organic state, believing that the people are like the cells of various organs, which is a physiological standpoint. I, however, have the idea of the organic nation, and stand from a biological point of view (in fact, Sun Yat-sen's nationalism is based on this, but people do not realize it). Because the existence of the people now is a continuation of the growth of their ancestors; reproduction is the continuation of life, and life is the development of life. Therefore, the people's responsibility is on the one hand to maintain the inherited qualities, and on the other hand to promote the function of evolution. This theory, explained in terms of universal physics, sees the former as centripetal force and the latter as centrifugal force. Only by having both of these forces simultaneously can the universe operate and have organization. Similarly, we need these two forces to cure the source of our nation's disease! Ignorance. As for how our nation maintains its inherited qualities? The inherent morality and inherent knowledge have long been lost, as others have already said, so there is no need to elaborate. How does our nation promote the function of evolution? In modern times, learning from Western civilization, such as training the army, has resulted in retreating in the face of foreign insults and going to civil war as if going to death, separating the country's territory, and declining national power. If we run schools, the result is to create batches of new-style bureaucrats and new-style young masters. If we learn sports,... with this situation, how can we avoid national destruction? But this is not my opposition to Western civilization, but rather my opposition to China only learning the superficial aspects of Western civilization, without knowing how to take the essence of Western civilization. Learning superficially results in [attempting to walk like Handan, crawling back]. Moreover, our country is already lagging behind the times, so how should we use the most economical method and follow the fastest path to obtain the true essence of modern civilization and catch up with the vanguard of the times?

Where lies the true essence of modern Western civilization?

One is the power of supply, and the other is the power of control. The so-called power of supply is to invent people's knowledge and technology, control nature, and produce raw materials for human evolution, which is the science of things. The so-called power of control is to guide the direction of people's knowledge and technology application, control society, and manage the finished products for human evolution, which is the science of people. Therefore, to obtain the true essence of Western civilization, we must put in practical effort to study hard and think deeply, without resorting to empty boasting and fanaticism. Indeed, China's shortcut to a way out lies in this.

If someone says that the true essence of Western civilization lies in sports, then I will have nothing to say. Montesquieu's misperception of British politics laid the foundation for modern democracy; the explanation of the Chu book by the Yan man, and the [烛] of the Yan man, could awaken King Zhao of Yan to seek talent. Perhaps sports may not be the path to China's prosperity, so why not let the people of the country rise up, use all their energy, and gather the power of the whole people to promote sports and implement sports. But I wonder what your opinion is?

Free Talk

[Ah Q's Likeness] 143

—

It seems that anyone who has read "The True Story of Ah Q" will never forget Ah Q's thoughts and consciousness? The essence of "The True Story of Ah Q" lies in the powerful revelation of this kind of "Ah Q's Likeness."

The main points of "Ah Q's Likeness" can be summarized as follows:

When actually failing or submitting, one has "spiritual victory" to comfort oneself, thus "turning defeat into victory," and sleeping soundly. Ah Q's famous sayings, such as "being beaten by his son" and "my ancestors are stronger than yours," are his philosophy of "spiritual victory."

When Zhao Mu'ye or Zhao Xiucai's big stick comes, he usually dares not resist; when the fake foreign devil's little [杕] comes, he also does not resist; but when those whom Ah Q considers his equals or juniors, such as Wang Hu and Little D, approach Ah Q like friends, Ah Q wants to assert his status and even wants to establish his authority, although the result is often only "spiritual victory," but Ah Q's "ambition" will never fade.

This is the so-called "Ah Q's Likeness," which is also the common likeness of most Chinese people who have been educated by the direct descendants of Yao, Shun, Yu, Tang, Wen, Wu, Confucius, and Mencius for thousands of years!

Since the publication of "The True Story of Ah Q," "Ah Q's Likeness" has been ridiculed by many people; but despite the ridicule, "Ah Q's Likeness" still manifests itself in the myriad social phenomena. Especially after the "September 18th" national crisis, the "spiritual victory" and "non-resistance" of "Ah Q's Likeness" can be said to have been brought into full play.

Then can "Ah Q's Likeness" also be said to be the national character of the Chinese nation? This is not necessarily the case! Because not all Chinese people with yellow faces are so incompetent. Haven't you seen the bloody battles of the Northeast Volunteer Army in the past year? The reason for this is probably that those Northeast people who joined the Volunteer Army have not received the inner teachings of the direct descendants of Yao, Shun, Yu, Tang, Wen, Wu, Zhou, and Confucius.

On this point, the alias of "Ah Q's Likeness" can also be called "Saint's Likeness" or "Adult's Likeness."

The Path of Culture 144

— Qian Gechuan

Zhu Dan I have a secret to tell you. I've fallen in love with a very noble woman, and I'd like you to help me out by writing a little note for me to throw in front of her.

Professor Very good!

Zhu Dan It must be written very beautifully, right?

Professor Of course. Do you want to write to her in poetry? Zhu Dan No, no; no poetry.

Professor Do you want to write only in prose?

Zhu Dan No prose, and no poetry.

Professor Then if you don't use prose, you have to use poetry.

Zhu Dan Why is that?

Professor Because when a person wants to express himself, he is limited to using prose or poetry.

Zhu Dan Is there nothing else besides prose and poetry?

Professor No. Everything that is not prose is poetry, and everything that is not poetry is prose.

Zhu Dan Then? What are we using when we speak?

Professor Prose.

Zhu Dan What? When I say, "Nicole, bring my slippers, bring me my nightcap," is that also prose?

Professor Exactly.

Zhu Dan Good heavens, I've been speaking prose for more than forty years, and I didn't even know it myself.

(Excerpt from a play by Molière)

Someone's Dream 145

— Ms. Cao Ruhui

Last night, he had a dream. Even now, the blurred and hazy dreamscape, like thin gauze, like light mist, is still faintly floating before his eyes. The dream was like this:

He didn't know when, but suddenly a pair of golden wings grew under his ribs, very large, like [垂天之] clouds. Flapping his wings, he rose from the ground very naturally, overlooking the earth in the vastness, in the clouds. It was rotating very quickly beneath him, making him dizzy and frightened, and finally he stopped on a high mountain of ten thousand [仭]. The mountain was in the clouds, on the horizon, in an unimaginable dreamscape. He stood proudly on the summit.

Look, how sublime he is! A light mist like thin gauze shrouded him, a colorful cloud floated above his head, the sun and moon smiled at him, and the stars twinkled at him. He occasionally looked down, and the ocean sang a clear song, worshipping at his feet; the smaller ones were like ants, like dust, tiny and insignificant. He occasionally laughed, and they all echoed his laughter. He occasionally became angry, and they were all terrified and trembled. Indeed, he stood above all, who knew how many thousands of millions of grains of dust had to accumulate to create this high mountain that reigned over all? So he sang and danced, as if victory and glory would forever belong to him. He despised everything, looked down on everything, trampled on everything. He thought that everything was insignificant and mediocre, only he was sublime and great. He arrogantly cast contemptuous glances around.

The days passed quickly, but also very slowly. He continued to laugh, dance, and sing!

One day, suddenly a tragic and loud song came from under his feet, from the underground layers, it was the chorus of thousands of people, and the lyrics were:

[We are dust, we are dust,]

We created the universe and the world, even this high mountain!! This towering throne was also accumulated from our flesh and blood. Look, that kid, that devil, how happily he sits on the summit!

We will forever endure the days under his throne. Brothers, we can no longer endure these days. Let's work together to throw that kid down, we want to be a free and equal grain of dust!

We want to create a free and equal world!] In this tragic song, a violent shock occurred under his feet, as if the sky was about to collapse, the earth was about to split, and a volcano was about to erupt. Along with this violent shock, he was tossed, dizzy, and confused. Immediately, he was furious, he shouted: [Stop, don't make noise, you beasts!]

But this scolding made the singing louder and the shock more violent, and finally the mountain collapsed, and like a dead dog, he rolled down from the summit. In his last breath, he still heard the loud song very clearly: [We want to be a free and equal grain of dust,] We want to create a free and equal world!] Last night, he had such a dream.

Yang Qiu Replies to [Yang Chun] 146

— Yang Qiu

Last month, in order to criticize the so-called [words] published in a certain insignificant publication, I casually wrote an article [Reading the Special Issue of the Liberation Movement of Words [After Respectful Feeling]] and submitted it to Free Talk for publication. Recently, a friend told me that someone named [Yang Chun] had published an article in that boring publication to defend someone named Zeng, the gist of which was that I did not point out the shortcomings of Zeng's so-called [words], and that Zeng's words [had received many praises from the sports world, and would become an immortal work], and vaguely referred to me as a [ruffian] and a [纨绔子].] I think [Yang Chun] is really too stupid, simply pitifully stupid. (Someone named Zeng seems to be smarter.) Now, I would like to respectfully copy Zeng's [words] (?) again, and re-copy my criticism of Zeng's words as follows, so that [Yang Chun] can see it clearly again.

Painted Hall Spring

The days begin to lengthen at the start of the year, guests come to comfort my desolation. Casual entertainment is harmless, playing mahjong. Drink up all the wine in the cup, what do I care about national affairs. There are still beautiful women before the wine vessel, but I can't go wild and count the chips.

Magpie Branch North is severely cold, not as warm as Jiangnan; the puppet state actually sees peace, how is it like the chaos in the Central Plains?

[The Plenary Session] was also held, but saving the country became a suspended case; all the officials who attended got official positions, and no one cared about the national crisis.

The above is a copy of Zeng's words, and my criticism is: When the days are long, one should [entertain] and [play mahjong]; when there are [beautiful women] before the wine vessel, why should one care about [not going wild] [being unable to go wild]? [The times] are [new], I am old-fashioned, what do I care [what do I care]! Those who praise me do not necessarily have to be stern, a sneer is enough for someone with a sense of shame, Yang Chun, why must you force me to expose all the words, making it difficult for Zeng?

To be honest, in terms of consciousness, these two pages of [words] vividly portray Zeng as a representative of [小白脸 culture]!! No, just a fake [薄儿], a lecherous degenerate youth. You see, during the Lunar New Year, Shanhaiguan was captured by the Japanese army, and the Northeast Volunteer Army was fighting bitterly with the imperialists in the freezing cold, but our self-proclaimed [writer] Zeng felt that the days were too [long] and life was too [凑凉] (!), so he could only find a way to [entertain]. Fortunately, [guests came], and with four feet gathered, they [played mahjong]. After the boredom of playing mahjong was gone, they also had to [drink wine]. When the wine was drunk and the mood was high, they shouted: [What do I care about national affairs]. After shouting, they saw that there was [beautiful women] in the same seat (meaning women). They could not help but be happy and their hearts throbbed, wishing they could [go wild] immediately, but perhaps because there were people around hindering them, they finally [could not go wild], so Zeng could not help but sigh with regret. You see, in these short forty-seven characters, is there not a [小白脸] who does not know anything!! No, is there not a lecherous prodigal's ugly state vividly present? Is there not the face of a most vulgar frivolous young man active in it? Secondly, in the first half of the [卜算子], the sentence [the puppet state actually sees peace, how is it like] the chaos in the Central Plains, in addition to expressing boring complaints, it also wipes out the Japanese imperialists' atrocities in the Northeast, as well as the heroic struggle of the Northeast Volunteer Army against imperialism. Is it formally acknowledging that the Japanese imperialists' seizure of our Northeast is absolutely correct, what is the intention? Yang Chun, is the puppet state really [peaceful]? I advise you to quickly follow Zeng to the puppet state to be a docile citizen under the [Pu Yi Sacred Heavenly Son's rule]! And this is also the most appropriate way out for you and Zeng!

Furthermore, in terms of technique, Zeng's [words] are even more [incomprehensible]. As for [words], I certainly oppose deliberately carving and 反對[巧], but what about the so-called [打打麻將], what do I care about national affairs, is that really a sentence? Are [words] [liberated] in this way? [牛溲馬] [勃] are all called [words], and they are actually printed and said to be [liberated words]. If we do not want this [有毒質的東西] to harm innocent young people, if we do not want [纨绔子] to make trouble in the literary world, is it not appropriate to give him a little lesson?

Finally, I must sincerely advise Yang Chun to calm his mind, and also advise Zeng to recognize the times, recognize himself, and from now on, read more books, do more meaningful things, brag less, and write less disgusting poetry. I have said everything here, and if you continue to be verbose, I will not reply again, so as not to waste the valuable space of Free Talk and my own valuable time.

Black Girl's Quest for God (14) 147

— By Sherwood Anderson, Translated by Yixian

At this time, she felt quite disillusioned with the old men; therefore, she left them, which made her very happy. She continued onward until she reached the shaded riverbank by the roadside; there, she saw fifty black people of her kind, who were evidently hired as porters. They were sitting down eating, separated by a considerable distance from a group of white gentlemen and ladies. The ladies were wearing shorts and cork helmets, and the black girl knew they were explorers, just like the men. They had just finished their meal. Some of them were dozing, and others were writing in their notebooks.

"What kind of expedition is this?" the black girl asked the leader of the porters.

"It's called the Curiosity Expedition," he replied.

"Are they good white people, or bad white people?" she asked.

"They are strange people, they don't mind making a fuss over small things," he said. "They ask questions just for the sake of asking questions."

"Hey! What are you doing?" one of the ladies called out. "Go away; you're not allowed to stop here. You'll distract the men."

"You're the same," the black girl said.

"Tch, girl," the lady said. "I'm fifty years old. I'm asexual. They're very familiar with me. You should go away."

"You don't need to worry: they aren't white people," the black girl said in a rather contemptuous tone. "Why do you call yourselves the Curiosity Expedition? What are you curious about? Are you curious about God?"

This remark elicited such a joyful burst of laughter that it woke up those who were dozing, and they asked others to retell the joke to them.

"Civilized people only started to have any curiosity about this question a few centuries ago," one of the gentlemen said. "It was before the fifteenth century, I think," another said. "Shakespeare was a complete atheist."

"Shakespeare can't be considered everyone," a third person said. "The national anthem is a product of the eighteenth century. Look, in it, we use God to do our dirty political work."

"That God is different," the second gentleman said. "In the Middle Ages, God was considered to be making us, teaching us to work incessantly. Once the bourgeoisie rose up, the feudal aristocracy overturned the obligations that had always been the price of their privileges, and people got a new God. This new God is used by the upper classes, teaching him to work incessantly. Destroy their politics; obstruct their conspiracies—do this, do that."

"Yes," the first gentleman said; "and then, there's the third one, the petty bourgeoisie's God, whose job it is to wipe the book clean on Sundays with his blood, when they fill it up during the week with their business frauds in the book of angels who record human good and evil."

"Both of these Gods are still in power," the third gentleman said. "If you have these doubts, then try replacing a suitable verse in the second verse of the national anthem; or try removing the confession of sins from the prayer book."

Ideal Rural Education (Part 2) Xu Zhengji 3. Supporting the Establishment of Agricultural Product Cooperatives. In recent years, the people who have been directly or indirectly exploited by capitalists are the villagers. Merchants have used every possible means of exploitation, so the phenomenon of "rural economic bankruptcy" has become unstoppable. We say "education is omnipotent," they say "education is the root of all evil." There are many sources of funding for the education sector that rely on the blood and sweat of farmers, and we should give them a strong arm out of compassion. "Agricultural product" cooperatives are a good way to free them from the monopoly of merchants and the exploitation of farmers. However, they do not understand the meaning and organization of cooperatives. Teachers in rural schools should promote and publicize the benefits of cooperatives. The Jiangsu Construction Department is very enthusiastic about the cooperative cause and has established cooperative instructors in various counties to specifically guide farmers' cooperative enterprises. This is indeed a good phenomenon. In the current economically bankrupt rural areas, obtaining this powerful assistance may be a boost to rural economic recovery.

4. Assisting in Organizing Rural Farmers' Defense Corps. In recent years, people's livelihoods have declined to the extreme, resulting in rampant bandits and people living in dire straits. Although local governments should bear the responsibility, farmers may as well arm themselves for self-defense. With peaceful neighborhoods, all undertakings can be carried out. If rural schools want to be the center of the community, this is also an important task.

In schools, organize Boy Scouts to give them a disciplined, militarized upbringing. Rural children have many opportunities to exercise their bodies. It is better to replace the gymnastics subject with Boy Scouts.

(4) How to Transform Rural Education

Past rural education has undoubtedly failed. This is due to pursuing quantity over quality. In the future, we should change our approach, "seeking quality over quantity," striving for economic concentration, employing good teachers, and being responsible for management. Existing rural primary school teachers should be selected by administrative authorities from specialized talents to preside over short-term training in order to achieve the realization of saving rural education and working together. Important News

Schools Should Pay Attention to the Ministry of Education's Regulations on Covering Reports with Seals

The Ministry of Education has formulated regulations for covering reports with seals on seal paper. In addition to ordering all educational institutions and universities directly under its jurisdiction, it has also issued a circular to the education departments of all provinces and cities, stating that the seals of institutions are used for identification and to show trustworthiness. The custody and use of seals are extremely important. In recent years, students applying to schools have often forged diplomas in the hope of deceiving the authorities. After being admitted, they are submitted to the Ministry for review and have been repeatedly discovered. This kind of bad behavior not only hinders the education system but also violates criminal law. The Ministry has always taken strict measures to crack down on this. Therefore, two types of seal paper for institutions and schools have been specially made. In addition to distributing them for completion, this circular, together with ○ copies of the seal paper form, is attached. The Department is ordered to immediately cover the seal paper for institutions with seals and distribute the seal paper for schools to the affiliated public and private secondary schools, instructing them to comply with the procedures together and submit them to the Ministry for filing. This order (1) This seal collection contains five copies: one copy is kept in the Secretariat of the Ministry, one copy is kept in the Higher Education Department, one copy is kept in the General Education Department, one copy is kept in the General Affairs Department, and one copy is filed.

(2) Education Departments and Bureaus of all provinces, Education Bureaus or Social Bureaus of municipalities directly under the Executive Yuan, and the Weihaiwei Management Office, etc., should cover five copies of the seal of the Department, Bureau, or Office on the institution seal paper and submit them.

(3) Each university should cover five copies of the university seal and the seals of each college and department of the university on the school seal paper and the school college and department seal paper. For example, Central University should cover five copies of the university seal, using five school seal papers, and also cover five copies of the seals of the Colleges of Liberal Arts, Science, Law, Education, and Agriculture, using ten school college and department seal papers. Example 2: Peking University should cover five copies of the university seal, using five school seal papers, and also cover five copies of the seals of the Colleges of Liberal Arts, Science, and Law, using five school college and department seal papers.

(4) Each independent college should cover five copies of the college seal on the school seal paper and submit them.

(5) Each specialized school should cover five copies of the school seal on the school seal paper and submit them.

(6) Each secondary school should cover five copies of the school seal on the school seal paper and submit them.

(7) Seal paper for national, provincial, and registered private specialized schools and above will be sent directly to the schools by the Ministry, and each school will report directly to the Ministry.

(8) Seal paper for public and private secondary schools in each province and city will be sent to the schools by the Ministry of Education Departments and Bureaus, and each school will submit them to the competent Department or Bureau for reporting to the Ministry.

(9) If the seal paper is insufficient, national, provincial, and registered private specialized schools and above may apply to the Ministry for requisition. If it is forwarded by the Education Department or Bureau, the Department or Bureau may copy and forward it according to the issued format and paper quality.

The above donation amounts are based on the actual salary issued by each organ. Service personnel and public servants should also be charged according to the standard; (4) the donations in each county and city should be collected by the person in charge of each organ in the county and city and remitted to each province; in each province or municipality directly under the central government, the donations should be collected by the person in charge of each organ in the province or municipality directly under the central government and remitted to the Central Aircraft Donation Custody Committee; (5) the Central Aircraft Donation Custody Committee should be organized by five to seven members designated by the Central Political Conference. In addition to sending a letter to the Central Executive Committee, it should be recorded and sent for reference. In accordance with this, in addition to issuing orders separately, the departments are ordered to comply and instruct all affiliated organizations to comply as well. Colleagues of the Vocational Education Society Formulate Measures for Concurrently Undertaking National Salvation Work 152

To be Implemented Immediately

The China Vocational Education Society, in view of the loss of the Northeast, and now with the outbreak of the Rehe War, believes that the rise and fall of the nation depend on it. This is a critical moment for the survival of the Chinese people. Therefore, it has joined forces with the office and all colleagues of the self-managed, agency-managed, and jointly managed institutions to formulate measures for concurrently undertaking national salvation work. The measures have been approved by the office staff meeting and will be implemented immediately. The progress of the work must be reported monthly for comparison. The measures are as follows: 1. All food and supplies must use domestic products and be widely encouraged in general society. The method of encouragement should be carried out according to local conditions. 2. Do not use Japanese goods. We have already taken an oath two years ago and should strictly abide by the oath. How to publicize this should also be considered according to local conditions. 3. Donate to the Northeast Volunteer Army. The amount does not matter, as long as it can be continued. Schools should use this to encourage students, and villages should use this to encourage farmers. The method of payment can be sent through the special department of the Society or sent to the bank. The names and amounts of all donors will be published in the Society's monthly report every month. 4. In all kinds of school-style education, for children, youth, or adults, in ordinary classes, when there is teaching material related to national culture or Sino-foreign relations, we should do our best to arouse national spirit. Outside of class, we should find ways to make students develop patriotic thoughts, expand national consciousness, and deepen national sentiment. Here are a few examples: (1) Hold weekly meetings to report on current events and lecture on national humiliations and national hatred; (2) Compose patriotic songs and have students practice singing them; (3) Compile and post wall newspapers, focusing on national hatred and national humiliation; (4) Compile and post pictures, focusing on national hatred and national humiliation; (5) Give a 5-minute speech before class, all about patriotism and national salvation. The words should be concise, refined, and stimulating, or do it during the first class of each day; (6) Introduce national heroes, compile stories and novels, or ballads, and have students read and sing them; (7) Guide defense organizations and carry out military training; (8) Pay special attention to cultivating young people who have special achievements and can be developed, so that they can become patriots. 5. In all kinds of social-style education, for the people being taught (especially farmers in rural areas), in addition to education on livelihood, science, etc., we should find ways to arouse patriotic feelings, explain the world situation, and train them in group life and cooperative habits. It may be worthwhile to make teaching about shame and war the main goal. The teaching materials and methods are roughly the same as the previous examples. 6. All colleagues of the institutions should use their usual enthusiasm for education, identify national salvation work as the only goal at present, and formulate a new kind of discipline for themselves in terms of self-cultivation, using money and objects, within and outside the scope of their duties, social interactions, and spare time (such as redoubling their efforts, being particularly frugal, reducing entertainment, and participating in patriotic movements, all of which can be specified one by one) to adapt to the current needs. It is advisable for everyone to write out these rules themselves for colleagues to consider and imitate. It is especially hoped that they will be able to write out their practical experience one by one in the future.

Health Education Committee, Health Group Meeting 153

Health Education Committee to Convene Tomorrow

Education Bureau Moves, Original Site to Become a Hospital

The Health Group of the Health Education Committee, organized by the Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau and the Education Bureau, held its second meeting in the Education Bureau's conference room on the 24th of last month. Committee members Li Ting'an, Pan Gongzhan, Wu Liguo, Tong Feicheng, Sun Jiaqi, and Zhou Shang attended. Director Li Ting'an chaired the meeting and performed the formalities. First, each committee member reported on the implementation of the previous motions, and then the following matters were discussed: (1) Approved the detailed rules for the group's office; (2) Approved the draft regulations for children's insurance; (3) Insurance for faculty and staff will be formulated separately later; (4) The Children's Day draft will be reviewed by Committee members Zhou Feicheng and Wu Liguo and submitted to the general meeting; (5) Existing good films should be used first for health inspection films, and then improved, to be discussed at the next meeting; (6) Committee member Wu Liguo is responsible for preparing health propaganda films; (7) After the Education Bureau moves to the San Shi Central District, the Education Bureau's buildings should be left for use as a small hospital and health insurance business, etc. The Health Education Committee is scheduled to hold its second general meeting tomorrow (2nd) at the Education Bureau to discuss implementation issues.

A Letter from Colleagues in the Shanghai Education Community to Colleagues in the National Education Community 154

The Education Community Should Lead by Example in Advocating for National Salvation and Resistance Against Japan

Recognize that All Educational Endeavors Take Patriotic National Salvation as Their Soul

Divide into Passive and Active Aspects, and Make Strenuous Efforts to Implement

Esteemed Colleagues in the National Education Community, the brutal Japanese militarists, indulging in their militaristic fervor, disregard all humanitarianism, justice, and treaties, occupy our land, slaughter our people. The puppet state of the Northeast has already been established, the scars of Shanghai have not yet healed, and now the war in Rehe has begun. To satisfy their insatiable greed, disturbing Tianjin and Peiping, and coveting the Yangtze River and the sea, are all within expectations. Our people, facing this desperate situation, have no choice but to rise up united, with the determination to die, seeking a new path to regeneration. What else is there to say?

In recent years, the government has been plagued by internal suppression of bandits and misled by external mediation, hesitating and indecisive, leading to the failure to recover lost territory. Our fathers, elders, brothers, sisters, and relatives in the three northeastern provinces have been groaning and suffering in captivity for years. This is truly an unprecedented humiliation. Righteous people weep blood and wish to sacrifice themselves; brave warriors sing mournful songs and think of killing the enemy. The hearts of the people of the nation are not all dead. In the Battle of Shanghai, loyalty and bravery were recognized worldwide, while the Northeast Anti-Japanese Volunteer Army rose time and again, sparing no effort to fight the brutal enemy with their flesh and blood, enduring hardships for more than a year. Their righteousness and benevolence have moved people far and wide. Now the government has resolved to resist the enemy, and a large army of over 200,000 is saving Rehe. The morale is high, and the pent-up feelings are waiting to be unleashed. Even poor farmers in remote areas provide supplies and transportation, even if it means bankruptcy, without complaint. Even elementary school students donate money and goods, ashamed to be behind others in patriotism. Judging from the manifestation of public sentiment, it is not difficult to predict the future of the nation.

What is concerning is that inland transportation is traditionally inconvenient, and the general public lacks organization. Therefore, the arousal of national sentiment, the expansion of national consciousness, and the strengthening and effectiveness of collective action all depend on the enlightenment and training of broad education. This is the responsibility of our colleagues in the national education community. To abandon the pen for the sword and rush to the front lines is indeed an urgent need of the moment, but this cannot be expected of everyone, nor is it necessary to expect it of everyone. In today's large-scale war and long-term resistance, the front lines rely on a large number of brave soldiers who sacrifice their lives on the battlefield, while the rear relies on a large number of organized people who are active in their communities, cooperating and working together to maximize effectiveness. In this extraordinary change, it is impossible to achieve anything by following old habits and living as usual. It is imperative that all the people of the country, whether farmers, workers, merchants, or scholars, regardless of who they are, should devote a portion of their daily work, resources, and energy to engaging in national salvation work in addition to their existing occupations, in order to reverse this critical situation. Our colleagues in the national education community should lead by example, personally advocating for it, recognizing that all current work must be centered on national salvation and resistance against Japan, that all undertakings must take national salvation and resistance against Japan as the pivotal point, and that all education must take patriotic national salvation as its soul.

Now, let us try to list concrete examples, hoping that our colleagues in the national education community will work together diligently and strive to implement them.

(1) In the passive aspect, we must eradicate the despicable mentality of complacency, change the bad habits of extravagance and laziness, eliminate the cruel and cold atmosphere of exclusion and suspicion, and redouble our efforts, frugality, diligence, and tolerance. Material enjoyment can be postponed to another day, and there is no need to dwell on trivial grievances.

(2) In the active aspect, we must encourage the courage to avenge our shame, inspire the spirit of chivalry and sacrifice, and motivate the national consciousness of the majority of people. We must strengthen their group organization and cultivate their arduous life. In classroom lectures, in addition to subjects such as civics and history, we must also devote a portion of the time to instilling patriotic thoughts. In extracurricular activities, in addition to gatherings and drills, we must also pay attention to their individual personalities, in order to cultivate aspiring people with ambition. As for the general public, we must also make contact and establish connections with them, participate in the organization of their patriotic groups, and assist in the progress of their national salvation work. As for those who specialize in mass education, they should take the awakening of the national soul as their only mission.

Now that the country has reached this point, who is to blame need not be investigated in detail. Our education community only feels immense shame and remorse and seeks to atone for our sins and strive to redeem ourselves. If we are unwilling to make efforts for even this minimum amount of national salvation work and continue to live in a drunken stupor, regarding the rise and fall of the nation as having nothing to do with us, how can we face our numerous students, our common people, and especially our soldiers who have died on the battlefield? Ask yourself, and reflect upon it. According to the Tianjin newspaper, a female storyteller named Li Xiangrong gives a five-minute patriotic speech before each performance to inspire the audience. In Germany, middle school students practice martial arts in the cold and snow, claiming that Germany is a nation disarmed by others and wishing to forge their bodies into plowshares and iron to clash with the enemy's guns and cannons. Our colleagues in the national education community, remember this, and deeply remember that the mentors who guide the people should not be inferior to a small female storyteller. Can we not feel ashamed in our hearts for the words and deeds of German middle school students? Saving the country is saving oneself, and everyone has a heart. Do not yield when it comes to benevolence, please start with yourself. We respectfully express our heartfelt thoughts, hoping that you will take note of them.

The Municipal Bureau of Education Sponsoring a Radio Broadcasting Tutorial Class 156

Broadcasting to Begin Tonight from 9:00 PM to 10:00 PM

In order to promote social education and facilitate the extra-curricular tutoring of workers and apprentices, the Municipal Bureau of Education is sponsoring a radio broadcasting tutorial class, lecturing on three subjects: [Civics], [Mandarin], and [English]. It has been repeatedly reported that one section of the lecture will be broadcast from 9:00 PM to 10:00 PM tonight. The class is now widely recruiting students. Anyone who wishes to take any of the subjects in this class, regardless of gender or age, can register at any time with the Fourth Section of the Municipal Bureau of Education on Daji Road, without a limit on the number of students and without charging fees. For registration procedures, you must bring two 2-inch half-length photos of yourself (if you do not have photos, you can first obtain a photo donation certificate from the Municipal Bureau of Education and have photos taken at the specially contracted photo studio for only 21 cents for every four photos), fill out the registration form, and the class will issue a student certificate, which will entitle you to be a student of the class. Students must provide their own textbooks. [Civics] and [Mandarin] textbooks are sold by the Datong Bookstore, purchased with a student ID card, and the donation photo is sold at 20% off the original price as a discount (the subscription is divided into two types: a full subscription to the Morning Post is specially priced at one yuan every two months, and a subscription to the lecture notes only is specially priced at one yuan and five cents per year). It is said that the Municipal Bureau of Education on Daji Road in Nanshi and the Hengsen Company broadcasting station in the Baoanfang on Nanjing Road have the class's training method available for consultation. In addition, since March 1, the tutorial class will broadcast lectures every Monday, Wednesday, and Friday (English), Tuesday and Thursday (Mandarin), and Saturday (Civics). The time is from 9:00 PM to 10:00 PM. All sectors that have installed wireless radios can listen to the broadcast freely at that time.
