Shanghai Middle School Affiliated Elementary School to Hold 30th Anniversary Celebration 158

On the morning of the 8th of this month

The Provincial Shanghai Middle School Experimental Elementary School, located on Shangwen Road, Xiaoximen, was founded in the 29th year of the Guangxu era of the Qing Dynasty, originally named the 22nd Shop Elementary School. Later, due to its perfect management, it was ordered by the province to be renamed the Affiliated Elementary School of Longmen Normal School. Afterwards, the Normal School repeatedly changed its name, and the school also changed its name accordingly, from the 2nd Affiliated Elementary School to the Shanghai Middle School Experimental Elementary School. It usually pays attention to the experiments of new education, so it has always been well-known in the elementary education community. It is recently learned that the school has reached its 30th anniversary since its establishment, and it has been decided to hold a commemorative ceremony on the morning of March 8th. Zhou, the Director of the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education, Jia Jiying, the founder of the school, and Yang Pingyu, the former principal, will be invited to deliver speeches, and Shen Yougan, Ni Shangda, Gan Yuyuan, Chen Bai, and other graduates of the school will give speeches to plan for future improvements. On the morning of the 9th, an alumni association will be held to gather alumni from past years and hold a commemorative meeting. On the afternoons of the 8th and 9th, there will be art exhibitions and costume propaganda to resist Japan and contribute to national salvation. Moreover, many famous elementary schools in Shanghai are old friends of Longmen, so the performers participating in the art exhibition include more than ten schools such as Wanzhu, Xicheng, Wuben, Jingye, Yangzhi, Shangwen, Feihong, Danhua, Shihua, and Rongzheng, gathering the essence of elementary schools in the city. It is sure to be wonderful. It is also reported that on the 8th and 9th, there will be several commemorative rooms for graduates of past years, displaying photos of graduates from the past 30 years, and various historical scenes such as the return of Qingdao and Jinan after the World War and the rushing out of Yuguan, to jointly awaken the spirit of common hatred. At the same time, a thick commemorative book for the 30th anniversary of the school's establishment will be printed and presented to the guests, detailing the changes in China's educational goals over the past 30 years, as well as the evolution of elementary school courses, which will be helpful for studying the history of modern Chinese education.

Shanghai Academy of Fine Arts Holds Board Meeting 159

Chairman Cai Yuanpei Welcomes New Directors

Planning to Build a New School Building and Art Museum

The Shanghai Academy of Fine Arts held a board meeting at the Bank Association the day before yesterday at 7:00 PM, convened by Chairman Cai Yuanpei, and welcomed the new directors Xi Zhesheng, Wu Tiecheng, Chen Gongbo, Liang Hancao, Zeng Zhongming, and Pan Gongru to join the meeting. The attending directors included Cai Yuanpei, Wu Tiecheng, Qian Xinzhi, Ji Gongchuo, Sun Zhesheng (represented by Li Zhaohuan), Wang Yiting, Jiang Wenyu, Wang Xiaolai, Gao Lu, and Liu Haisu. Guests included Wang , Wu, Zheng Hongnian, Shen Xinqing, Li Zhaohuan, Li Dachao, and Wang Jiyuan, the Vice President of the school. Chairman Cai Yuanpei first delivered a speech to welcome the new directors and reported the purpose of the meeting, stating that the Academy of Fine Arts bears the mission of promoting our country's inherent culture and absorbing new foreign arts. The society has high expectations, and although the scale has been roughly formed in the past 20 years, the colleagues dare not be complacent about this and should continue to work hard to promote social evolution. Now that the original school building is not enough for application, it is planned to build a new school building and art museum on the Xujiahui base to build a cultural foundation. Then, President Liu Haisu reported on the current status of school affairs and future development plans, and read aloud Chairman Cai Yuanpei's own inscription on the initiation of the construction of the school's new school building and art museum, which was unanimously approved, and the committee charter was revised. A committee for planning the construction of the new school building and art museum was organized on the spot, and Cai Yuanpei, Sun Zhesheng, Wu Tiecheng, Qian Xinzhi, and Ye Gongchuo were elected as the presidium of the committee. All the directors, Zheng Hongnian, Wang Yunwu, Li Zhaohuan, Shen Xinqing, and Li Dachao were also invited to be members of the committee. During the meeting, the directors discussed in detail and unanimously stated that the school is the birthplace of China's emerging arts. It is urgent to build a new school building on the original base. The committee should actively raise funds to see the completion soon.

Tonight at 8:00 PM, Women's Basketball Game: Liangjiang vs. Western League 161

Location... Chinese Basketball Room

Spirits Rise After Three Losses

See if We Can Win Tonight

The Liangjiang Women's Basketball Team has been competing with Western teams for days and unfortunately lost. The Chinese people are disappointed because the team is about to travel to Europe and the United States. However, according to reliable information, the team members are not all going abroad. The Liangjiang School authorities are very cautious about the selection of team members who will go abroad and are still in the process of selecting. According to people in the sports world, there are three main reasons for Liangjiang's failure in recent days: (1) The Liangjiang team won the Western Youth Basketball Championship, and this time the Western Youth teams are determined to seek revenge and fight bravely. The Liangjiang team has no prejudice, so it cannot compete with the enemy. (2) The Liangjiang team is a newly formed team with only half a year of training. It is not as experienced as the old team, and it has always won battles and rarely failed. Its combat experience is still lacking, so it cannot cope with setbacks. (3) The Liangjiang team has had too much time for practice and competition recently, resulting in excessive fatigue of the team members. It is not that Liangjiang's technique is inferior to when it won the Western Youth Championship. However, the Liangjiang team members are focused on practice, and winning or losing is what they consider, so they are not discouraged by this. Tonight, they are scheduled to compete with the Western All-Star Women's Basketball League again. The time is still 8:00 PM, and the location has been changed to the Chinese Basketball Room in the French Concession. Tickets are 60 cents each. This competition is the last of Liangjiang's recent friendly competitions with Western teams, and the opponent is the elite of the Federation. The female athletes of Liangjiang are determined to fight hard. Moreover, this year's International Basketball Tournament will start this week, and the Liangjiang team members have all been selected as members of the Chinese national team, and the Federation team will also participate in the competition, so this match is no less than a preliminary competition between the Chinese national team and the Federation team.

Hankou City Unauthorized Holding of Regional Tournament

Shi Xinglong and Others Prepare to Build a Heated Swimming Pool, Construction to Begin Soon 169

Mr. Wang Xiaolai Appointed as President

Swimming enthusiasts Shi Xinglong, Li Rongyao, Yin Yanjun, Ling Chongju, Yu Binqi, Wang Jianxin, Hong Zunshan, Li Ziyu, and members of the Chinese Swimming Research Association are preparing to build a heated swimming pool inside the Huang Ke Gymnasium on Seymour Road in this city, as reported previously. However, due to unsuitable designs, several revisions were made. Now, the final design has been drafted and will soon be approved. Construction is expected to begin within two weeks and be completed within three weeks. Before completion, they plan to recruit 300 basic members, each paying a fee of ten yuan (divided into two installments), to enjoy one full year of membership rights. The association is dedicated to promoting swimming and training talent, with no profit motive. All operations will be transparent. Information is available in the bylaws, which will be sent upon request. The temporary office is located at Room 301, 9 Hankou Road, inside the China Industrial Development Corporation. Mr. Wang Xiaolai has been invited to serve as the president of the association.

Commercial News and Finance

The Current Situation and the Exchange Market

Gold Price Falls by Three Taels and Eight Mace

Large Bars Shrink, High Quotes Cause Panic, Eventually Lowered. Although the gold market opened well yesterday, public uncertainty and the deteriorating situation had an adverse impact on the market. As a result, prices fell. The exchange market also hardened. In the morning market, foreign telegrams indicated that London large bars had suddenly shrunk by 125 in both near and far terms. New York silver prices remained unchanged, but forward silver prices fell by more than 2%. Bank private cables then decreased by 0.1875, and the exchange market opened tighter than the previous close. The gold market then jumped to open at 774 taels and one mace. It was initially stable, and the exchange market was also good. Banque Belge pour l'Étranger and McCallum first closed June US dollars at 9.1875 and 9.25, so it once rose to 6 mace. The Hongkong and Shanghai Banking Corporation's quotes for both sterling and US dollars remained unchanged, but a downward trend was observed. Citibank offered April US dollars at 9 yuan, and June at 9.3125 was not easy to sell, so it dropped to 70 taels. After entering the market, even 9.375 was difficult to get out, and it fell to 68 taels and three mace, closing at 769 taels and eight mace. In the early morning, the opening price was 770 taels and nine mace due to the residual momentum of the noon close. The exchange market also showed some improvement, and banks were trading April US dollars at 9 yuan, once rising to 2 taels and 4 mace. However, the situation quickly deteriorated, sellers were very active, and public suspicion was heavy, leading to a downward trend. As a result, the exchange market also hardened. June gold traded at 9 yuan and a half before buyers appeared. Da Xing Yong fiercely sold, and only when it reached 66 taels and six mace did it start to rebound. Telegrams from Bombay reported a drop of more than ten annas, then a rise to more than 9 taels. However, the market still could not recover. No one wanted June US dollars at 9 yuan and a half, so it was lowered to 766 taels and a half, closing at 767 taels. The trend did not look promising and there was still volatility. Although the Central Bank intervened with spot sales, it was at a time of decline, and the amount was small, making it difficult to effect change. Shanghai Clearing House added eleven and a half taels. Swaps for March and April were priced at 3 taels to 3.41. It was observed that the market was chaotic during the day due to public panic, with sellers dominating. The market conditions for the day are recorded below.

The morning opened with a jump to 774 taels and two mace, a rise of 3 taels and four mace from the previous close, then to 4 taels. The exchange market also opened tighter than the previous close. Recent prices for sterling exchange were one shilling eight pence and one-eighth of a penny, and US exchange was 8.75. Hengxing was the first to buy bars, adding to 4 taels and seven mace. Yuanheng Hengyu came to sell, retreating to 3 taels and nine mace. Banque Belge pour l'Étranger bought June gold at 9.1875, Qingfa Yong bought bars, reaching 5 taels. Da Decheng Zhifeng Yong further bought, reaching 6 taels. Yu Hengyu came to sell, dropping to within 2 taels, to 4 taels and six mace. McCallum still closed June US dollars at 25, rising again to 5 taels and four mace. The Commodity Exchange then came to short sell, falling to around 4 taels. Jiuyin Feng offered June shillings at 25, but because Yuanmao Yong had once come to buy, there was still a struggle. By the time June US dollars were difficult to sell, Zhaofeng Chang came to sell, breaking to within 4 taels. The Hongkong and Shanghai Banking Corporation's quotes for both sterling and US dollars did not change, but fell further. Da Xing Yong was selling, and Hengxing also sold, falling to 1.18 taels. Citibank also offered April US dollars at 9 yuan. Retail investors absorbed some, slightly improving by a few qian. Yuancheng Yong offered more, and the exchange market had hardened. A Glimpse of the Competition in the Money Industry Market Before the Implementation of Abolishing Cents 173

Those Who Had Too Much Foreign Currency But Not Enough Silver Hastened to Sell

Afternoon Agreed Prices Were Collected by the Reserve

Abolishing the foreign cent was inevitable, but the date had already been decided to be implemented on March 1st (today), so yesterday, money houses, silver firms, and banks with excess foreign currency and not enough silver or excess silver and not enough foreign currency had to fully balance their positions yesterday to avoid difficulties in temporary allocation. The situation in the early and noon markets yesterday is recorded separately below. (Early market) Money houses, industry colleagues, and banks generally had excess foreign currency to sell, because the current market was flooded, and the cent price had a real possibility of falling. Now, restricted by the standard price, unable to reduce it, they all sold, but without a buyer, they had to compete fiercely with each other. As a result, Fuyuan Jiang came forward to buy as much as possible, but the cent price still had to be set at 7 qian 1 fen 5 li. The foreign currency bought by Fuyuan Zhuang was no less than 2,000,000, and each of the Central, China, and Jiaotong banks distributed tens of thousands, so the early market passed stably. (Noon market) There were even more sellers, and Fuyuan continued to receive at first, but by half past one, it had exceeded 1,000,000, and the sellers were still crowded, so they stopped buying, and the market suddenly stalled, unable to close. The industry association had to convene a temporary executive supervisory committee to discuss the day's methods, agreeing that all colleagues who wanted to sell in the noon market would be bought by the money industry reserve at the market price minus 1 hao 2 hu 5, and if colleagues wanted to buy, they would also be priced at 7.14875. Once this order was issued, the colleagues rushed to buy, so the reserve sold 1,670,000, and the noon cent price was set at 7 qian 1 fen 4 li 8 hao 7 hu 5. It was already half past three when the market closed.

New York's Financial Market 174

New York, February 27th, Telegraph. The improvement in the banking situation last weekend made those selling gold dollars increasingly dominant. Today, foreign exchange was consistently firm, and the franc has risen to a position where it is profitable to transport cash to France by ship.

The money market turned firm today. Although the short-term discount interest rate is still 1%, transactions outside the market cannot be completed at this price. Bank loan interest rates have risen by 1.5%, which is due to demand and unwillingness of banks to balance directly.

The Kercheval case empowers the financial administrator with supreme authority over national banks. His authority can urgently dispose of bank liquidity and limit withdrawal limits according to recent withdrawals and average deposit limits. This method can prevent banks from suspending withdrawals, like the Michigan crisis.

Foreign firms unloaded a large amount of futures for February. The total number of deliveries yesterday reached more than 800 boxes, mostly Italian goods.

80 Pieces of Chinese Silk Shipped to England 187

The British mail ship, Sumanli (蘇曼理) set sail yesterday morning carrying 80 pieces of yellow and white silk from Anli (安利) and other local firms to England.

Hardware: Thin Tinplate Gradually Improves 188

Yesterday's hardware market showed mixed performance. Tinplate, black iron sheet, new lead wire, tinplate tiles, and small split nails showed signs of active sales. New foreign silver, bundled steel, new coiled steel, edge nails, large bars, etc. remained depressed. In terms of prices, tinplate increased by 20 cents, selling for 12.5 taels (90 pounds), and 200-pound double-linked iron opened at 29.5 taels (up 20 cents). There were few fluctuations in other goods. However, thin tinplate in the tinplate category was unusually firm yesterday. Therefore, locks and the market are showing signs of improvement. The current spot goods of the same industry are limited, and future arrivals are far away, so the estimated prices have risen to 95 cents (6 feet) and 1.14 taels (7 feet). It was found that the domestic rivers and the various Changjiang firms were very interested yesterday, so the transaction volume reached as high as 5,000 to 6,000 sheets. It is said that the Fujian Ningbo firms have also been inquiring in recent days, and the market is expected to rise and not fall.

Essays

Cutting 189

-- Zhan Lu

Suppose the world is a vast and boundless garden, with the large and small countries built on it like famous and exotic flowers planted in separate areas. Each has its own characteristics and advantages in color, fragrance, and posture. The flower beds are their territory, and the fences are their national defense lines. As long as flowers and flowers, grass and grass, respect each other's territorial integrity and do not break through each other's national defense lines, then the world's peaceful garden will certainly not have any unfortunate wars.

To maintain this peaceful garden, it is essential to prevent the possibility of weeds growing inside [Mans, difficult to plan for], this ancient saying means that people with ambitions are as terrible as weeds. Now, everyone hates ambitious countries, aren't they the world's pests? In South Manchuria, no one cut them off, and they spread to Central Manchuria and North Manchuria. Recently, they have intensified and spread to Yuguan and Jehol. If it is allowed to spread continuously, it will spread to the entire territory of China, and of course it will also spread to all countries in the world. Then, wouldn't the peaceful garden I described turn into a field of weeds?

The League of Nations General Assembly passed the report of the Nineteen-Nation Special Committee by a vote of forty-two to one, as if it were wielding a blade of justice and cutting at the power. However, with only one cut, its evil hatred still exists, and it is not known whether the old roots will sprout again in the future, or grow faster than before the cut. How should this be dealt with?

After cutting the weeds, the second step should be to remove its evil roots. The Zuo Zhuan says: "Sever its roots, do not allow it to be planted, then the good will flourish." However, the power of the forty-two countries is only applicable to the word "cut" and cannot talk about severing its roots. Why? The writing of the number forty-two is exactly the word "cut." I think that the forty-one countries, apart from a "cut" for the world's weeds, are afraid that there are no other effective methods.

Puppets and the Like of Anti-Chen Ping 190

-- Si Su

In the midst of the invading cries of violent Japan, the word "puppet" suddenly came into being, and almost every newspaper in the country, large and small, cannot do without it every day. In terms of the word puppet itself, is it considered to be successful or frustrated? It is also worth studying. Originally, everyone regarded the word puppet as a synonym for puppet shows, and there was no qualification to be put in newspapers. Puppet shows are stringed puppet shows. There are also several specialized performances in Shanghai, called what Sheng Wutai, Xin Wutai, which can be found in the entertainment list of major newspapers. It is not like Tianchan, Samsung, etc., with famous actors. After spending money to watch the show, you can write a drama review and put it in the newspaper. Who would be happy to comment on stringed puppet shows? Even if it is commented on, it has no value to be published. Therefore, before September 18th, it was really difficult to find puppets in the newspaper. After September 18th, it suddenly came into being, and newspapers kept reporting it. In itself, this must be considered a period of showing off, and one must be very happy! However, it is not so. If the puppet itself is conscious, it will never be happy. Unless the puppet has forgotten its ancestors, it will shamelessly regard this moment of excitement as its own happiness! Because the puppet's ancestor once performed the glorious meritorious service of "preserving the Han and repelling the barbarians." Yuefu Zalu says; "When Emperor Gaozu of the Han was surrounded by Maodun in Pingcheng, one side of the city was Maodun's wife, Que Shi, with strong soldiers on three sides, and the fortress was starving. Chen Ping visited and learned that Que Shi was jealous, so he made wooden puppets with organs and danced in the city walls. Que Shi was worried that if she attacked the city, Maodun would definitely accept prostitutes, so she withdrew his troops. Later, musicians turned it into a plaything, which is the puppet." Don't underestimate the puppet, it can lift the siege of Pingcheng and preserve the Han Dynasty. Today's puppets are doing the opposite, becoming the minions of the enemy, and dividing up the territory of the Han Dynasty. Are they doing this willingly? I am afraid not. Puppets are still puppets. However, those who make them are not Chen Ping, but the likes of Zheng Xiaoxu, Xi Qia, and Zhang Haipeng. The use of puppets is the opposite of those made by Chen Ping! Perhaps the puppet already understands that the excitement in front of them is only temporary, and they will be put away after a while and will no longer be seen in the newspaper. The likes of anti-Chen Ping are still dreaming, mistakenly thinking that joy can be prolonged!

Youth 191

-- He Chonglou

Is the Time of Creation

Youth, the color of grass, the active spring, symbolizes the period of people's youth. If we consider "spring" as the plan of a year, then "youth" is the plan of people's lives.

"Flowers fall and can bloom again, youth never returns." This is the feeling of most young people who worry about their youth being fleeting. Because of this feeling, it is easy to go down the road of indulging in pleasure, and as a result, their youth will perish even more quickly!

A person must make good use of their youth, because although youth is the shortest, it is the most powerful. We must know that "praise" or "lament" do not recognize the value of youth itself. Only by raising the hands of the masses, grasping the times, and creating great undertakings can we not fail to live up to the precious youth.

Friends: Do not hesitate, shoulder your responsibilities, and work hard to move forward!

Impressions of a Barbershop 192

-- Fei Ming

Shanghai is worthy of being a mysterious city with terrible temptations. As long as you pay attention everywhere, you will find scenes that you have never seen or heard of anywhere, and you will realize everything about life, society, and even the world from this. A barbershop is a place that is often easily overlooked but is filled with abundant information about life.

Indeed, barbershops in Shanghai can keep up with barbershops in many major cities in the world. Compared with barbershops in famous cities such as Moscow and Tokyo, not to mention anything else, just in terms of equipment and service, they have already surpassed them.

Naturally, there are various grades of barbershops in Shanghai. Personally speaking, I have visited barbershops ranging from one dime to one dollar. Sometimes I feel that cheaper barbershops can even give me an unexpected satisfaction than fancy barbershops.

However, to be honest, I still prefer to go to barbershops that are less ostentatious, for reasons that are difficult to explain in a word.

On that Sunday evening, rather than saying that I went to get a haircut, I might as well say that I went to find some material for writing short essays. I broke into a first-class barbershop on Avenue Joffre.

Through the door, which released a wave of sweet and spicy perfume, I was led upstairs by the waiter. Unexpectedly, there was only me upstairs.

A smell of alcohol spewed out of the mouth of the barber, who was not wearing a mask, and I began to feel an unpleasant disappointment. [Bo Ai] sent over a small newspaper, and I sniffed it randomly. At this moment, with the sound of the upstairs bell, a wave of high-heeled leather shoes came up. Looking in the wall mirror, I saw three modern beauties with swirling smiles, led by the waiter to their seats. The fragrance in the room became even stronger.

Perhaps because I was the only member of the opposite sex among the customers present, I felt a kind of inexplicable joy. Driven by curiosity, I calmly observed the facial expressions of the three modern beauties in the mirror, and at the same time paid attention to listening to their laughter. Only then did I learn that they were going to participate in a charity performance to raise money to help the volunteer army.

Another unpleasant bell led up one or two drunken, fat foreign junior officers. They caught sight of the three Chinese modern beauties and revealed an extraordinary smile. From their conversation, it seemed that they heard a sentence: "Chinese women with a Western flavor." I silently thought: Why can't Westerners generally get rid of the image of bound feet when they imagine Chinese women?

Gradually, the dark hair in the mirror was waving. In another mirror, two pairs of unfamiliar green drunken eyes were peeking diagonally at the right side. My sensitive nerves seemed to be afraid that the female compatriots next to me would be attacked by unexpected misfortune, and I was willing to sit in the middle as their barrier.

The piercing whistling sound of a foreign tune began to become sharper. I suddenly saw that there were several strands of hair on the white cloth draped over my chest that spelled out the word "woman."

On the way home, I purely and secretly blessed the three hair-cutting girls!

Miscellaneous Remarks

Nine Flavor Tea 193

-- Zhang Yian

It is easy to describe the characters in a drama, but it is difficult to describe the real-life characters in society; because the characters in the drama are particularly exaggerated, and their characteristics are easy to see, while the characteristics of the real-life characters in society are not easy for you to see.

It is easy to describe the personality of Westerners, but it is difficult to describe the personality of Chinese people, because Westerners can often show their own personality, while Chinese people regard dissolving their own personality into the commonality of ordinary people as a kind of morality.

It is easier to describe the illiterate class characters in China than to describe the intellectual class characters, because in China, the intellectual class characters are good at hiding their egos, and the closer they are to cold and stiff things. (In fact, cold and stiff characters are not necessarily knowledgeable, and many are deliberately becoming cold and stiff, with unchanging expressions to show themselves as gentlemen.)

If you can pay attention to the grammar commonly used by ten people, you can find ten different language habits. Not only are the tones, words, and usage of words different, but even the organizational methods have their own personalities. Local environment and education level are probably the more important reasons.

Everyone inevitably has cheesy thoughts, but those who are more [elegant] will use their more [elegant] language to express them; those who are [more vulgar] will only use their more [vulgar] language and behavior.

A hypocritical and evasive person often has a stereotyped and unchanging expression. When he is socializing with people, he will show this unchanging expression.

Unmarried people always want to find a so-called lifelong partner, while married people cannot help but long for and reminisce about the freedom of single life.

At breakfast, I thought of something, and at the time I felt it was quite interesting, but I didn't record it. After the meal, I forgot to write it down. Later, when I tried to recall it, I completely forgot what it was. I don't know how many things like this that flash and disappear have been let go. In the future, if I feel something, I should write it down immediately.

Most of the people in Shanghai are smart. Even if they were not very smart originally, they would become too smart after being influenced by what they see and hear for a long time. However, I don't know what benefits this style of smart people has for the country and society.

Future education should pay attention to the correspondence between hands and brains, especially to the use of both hands. Scientific experiments and research, and industrial practice, must be done by hand. Thinking in vain, writing articles in vain, speaking in vain, shouting slogans in vain... the result is just in vain.

Schools in our country pay too little attention to the students' two hands, and their brains have not developed properly, which wastes many functions that should have been produced.

Emotions and thoughts are human, everyone has them, but it may not be possible for everyone to concretize them and say them or write them out.

The four corners of the tram car are the most coveted by passengers. When passengers are competing to sit in the corner seats, you can roughly understand the reason why warlords want to fight for territory. When passengers no longer compete to sit in the corner seats, I believe the warlords will no longer fight for territory. People have the habit of worshiping idols, and even more the ability to use idols. Some people respect creation and despise imitation. I think creation and imitation are connected. Creation is certainly valuable, but imitation is not to be blamed. From birth to adulthood, a person cannot get rid of going through many imitations. If imitation is blocked, there will be no learning, at least everyone will create a language that no one else can understand. If all imitation is blocked, then the result will inevitably become a primitive state. However, imitation should be regarded as a means of creation, which should be admitted.

Fiction

Landlord Tian 194

— Qin Shouou

Grandfather said, "We are not going back! Quickly destroy the bridge!" Indeed, judging from the current situation, if no one was willing to sacrifice their lives to resist the Japanese across the river, the wooden bridge would never have a chance to be destroyed; if the wooden bridge was not destroyed, Tianjia Village would immediately be trampled into flat ground by the Japanese. Therefore, when Xiaoling charged across the bridge, she did not plan to return.

Landlord Tian also knew the importance of this bridge, and the sacrifice of his two young grandchildren was even more clearly an inevitable fact. So, after closing his eyes and riding his horse across the bridge, he resolutely ordered the fifth son, hiding in the inner room, to immediately destroy the wooden bridge.

At the same time, the Japanese had divided into two groups, encircling Xiaohe and Xiaoling like dumplings.

Across the river, the old man straightened his back, sitting upright on his horse like a zombie, his eye sockets widened as much as possible, almost to the point of cracking; the water on his face, in the dim twilight, gleamed brightly, but no one knew whether it was sweat or tears; and even those two iron arms, wielding knives and swords and killing like hemp, could not stop trembling.

The Japanese were temporarily not preparing to rush into the river, determined to first deal with these two young martyrs who took death as the price for killing. A chaotic sound of killing shook the wilderness. Initially, people on this side could still vaguely see two things like wheels in the heavy encirclement of the Japanese, constantly rolling, rising, and colliding actively; sometimes they could even hear the wails of the Japanese after being shot, and the tragic and passionate roars of Xiaoling and Xiaohe... Gradually, the sound of the Japanese killing overwhelmed everything, and the forest-like array of knives was no longer seen moving.

The night wind passed through the willow forest, making a long howl like a monkey's cry, as if mourning the little warrior who was unyielding until death.

"Ah! Father! We can't just sit by and watch without saving them!" The fifth son, the only one remaining uninjured among the Tian family's soldiers, could not bear it and pleaded with Landlord Tian in a hoarse voice, advocating that everyone charge across the river again to rescue Xiaoling and them.

"No! No! No!" Landlord Tian tried his best to hold onto his wildly beating heart, endured all the pain, and burst out with an extremely resolute answer from between his teeth. (Seven)

Fierce Battles on the Lingnan Front Lines 195

Tang Yulin's Arrival at the Front Greatly Boosts Morale

Fierce Battle at Baishizui Lasts Three Days and Nights, Enemy Fails to Succeed

Seven Japanese Aircraft Destroy Many Civilian Houses in Lingnan

(Beiping) This morning, enemy troops continued to shell our positions in the Baishizui area, and our troops are still resisting desperately. (1st Dispatch)

(Beiping) Qin Island, 8 AM on the 1st: The Suzuki and Hattori Brigades are attacking our positions at Baishizui with intense artillery fire, and aircraft are bombing our Shaomao Mountain. However, due to the trenches built along the mountain, there was no damage. The fierce battle has lasted for three days and nights without success. In addition, the Miyama unit, under the cover of artillery fire, plans to rush to build positions outside Baishi Gate. Our army attacked fiercely with mortars, and their new position ultimately failed. (1st Dispatch)

(Beiping) Chengde, 4 PM on the 28th: The Shaomao Mountain area on the southern route was still in fierce battle on the morning of the 28th. The enemy heavily bombarded our positions with heavy artillery, and our troops guarded the key points, condescending from a high position, and resisted calmly. When the enemy approached, they were swept by machine guns, killing many. After holding out until noon, the Japanese army could not hold out and retreated. The enemy headquarters moved to Lijiabao on the 28th. The rebel Japanese troops in Suizhong and Jiukou arrived at Baishizui to reinforce on the 28th. Our rear troops also arrived at the front line, boosting morale. Seven enemy aircraft flew to Lingnan County again on the morning of the 28th and dropped more than ten bombs, destroying many civilian houses. They were repelled by our army using anti-aircraft guns. (1st Dispatch)

(Beiping) Chunhuang Island, Noon on the 28th: There were still fierce battles in the Lingnan area from 8 AM on the 28th. Japanese aircraft bombed Mutoucheng around 11 AM on the 28th, destroying many civilian houses. More than a thousand enemy troops were discovered in the Lishan area and were repelled by a certain brigade of our army. (1st Dispatch)

(Beiping) Chengde, 9 PM on the 28th: Chairman Tang Yulin went to Lingyuan front at 6 AM on the 28th to supervise the troops. Commander Sun Dianying went to the Chifeng front line at 3 PM on the 27th to command. (1st Dispatch)

Tang Yulin Goes to Lingyuan to Supervise Troops 196

(Beiping) Tang Yulin went to Lingyuan to supervise troops in the morning, and Sun Dianying went to Chifeng to command on the 28th. (28th Dispatch) (Beiping) Tang Yulin stated that he would not allow the Japanese to obtain Rehe until all the Chinese were dead. Retreating to the new defense line was a predetermined plan. (1st Dispatch)

(Beiping) Morale was greatly boosted after Tang arrived at Lingyuan and Sun Dianying arrived at Chifeng to supervise the troops, and they decided to immediately attack the enemy. (Dispatch)

(Beiping) Tang Yulin arrived in Lingyuan on the night of the 28th and immediately summoned Meng Zhaotian, Dong Futing, and military officers to discuss military strategies. The content was secret. Tang will inspect the foremost front line again. (1st Dispatch)

The Japanese concession is everywhere with barbed wire, but they demand that we protect the lives and property of Japanese residents. The situation is no different from the previous Tianjin Incident, but we are fully prepared and will be able to cope with ease. (Morning Central News Agency on the 1st)

Enemy Ships from Qinhuangdao and Harbin Approach the Coast of Shihe 199

Each Ship Flies a Battle Flag, Situation Serious

Rumor that a Japanese Aircraft Carrier Arrived at Qinhuangdao

(Tianjin) Eight enemy ships from Qinhuangdao, one or two of which occasionally spied on the Hebei River estuary in Beidaihe Bay, all approached the coast of Shihe on the morning of the 1st. Each ship was four or five li apart, with the head to the east and the tail to the west, flying battle flags, the situation is serious. The combat preparations of the Japanese army stationed in Tianjin have become acute. The lights in the city and suburbs were suddenly dim on the night of the 28th, and the Public Security Bureau immediately stepped up its guard. It was later found that the power transfer station was damaged. (1st Dispatch)

Part of them are said to be opening Jiukou. Two more Japanese ships arrived in the Qinhuangdao sea on the morning of the 28th, reaching a total of ten ships including the previous ones. Rumors in Qinhuangdao port make the situation extremely tense. The Japanese army in Shihe had no action on the 28th. (1st Dispatch)

Japanese Troops Parade in the Streets

And Deploy Defensive Works

At night, they took candles to the streets to read the wall newspapers. However, because there was a war with Japan but no severance of diplomatic relations, many Japanese people patrolled back and forth on the streets or at the east and west railway stations, inquiring about news. The Japanese troops also paraded in the streets, with an arrogant attitude, which was eye-catching. Yunnan Province Raises National Salvation Donations 211

Educational Circles Pledge One Million

The Yunnan National Salvation Association was established in Kunming to raise national salvation donations. The educational circles voluntarily pledged Yunnan currency of one million yuan. The allocation method is as follows: (1) 300,000 yuan will be pledged from the local education funds of various counties (1/10 of the total annual income). (2) 500,000 yuan will be pledged from the provincial education funds. (3) 200,000 yuan will be pledged by students throughout the province (1 yuan will be pledged by each elementary school student, 10 yuan by middle school students, and 20 yuan by university students). (Morning Central News Agency Dispatch on the 28th)

British Arms Embargo Apparently Shows Partiality 212

Treating Aggression and Self-Defense Equally Suits Japanese Scheming

The Previous Ban Will Be Reimplemented

Aircraft Are Also Included in the Ban

(London) As a result of the British government's decision to prohibit the transportation of arms to belligerent countries in the Far East, the 1931 Order in Council prohibiting the export of military equipment will be implemented. All aircraft and engines, whether assembled or disassembled, whether civilian or military, are included in the ban. Officials explained that the reason for classifying all types of aircraft into one category is that it is difficult to distinguish which aircraft are for peaceful purposes and which are for war purposes. (Special Dispatch from the Zi Lin Daily on the 28th)

The British Government Seeks International Cooperation 213

If There Is No Response, This Ban Will Be Changed

Our Charge d'Affaires in Britain Visits Simon to Exchange Views

(London) Responsible parties announced tonight that the British government's decision to prohibit the transportation of arms to the Far East is still not of any definite nature at present. The government is continuing to contact other governments through diplomatic channels. If a common agreement can be established by all countries, then the United Kingdom's own actions will be transferred according to the public actions of various countries. Conversely, if it is not possible to obtain the unanimous agreement of all countries, then the British Cabinet will consider within what limits the decision to prohibit the transportation of arms to the Far East should be changed. After all, this ban is originally meant to set an example. If other countries cannot be made to follow suit, then it is better to change it. (Havas Dispatch on the 28th)

(London) Chen Weicheng, the Chinese representative in Britain, discussed the arms embargo with Foreign Secretary Simon today. They exchanged views on the current situation in Rehe, the relationship between China and Britain, and especially the problems of the three northeastern provinces. However, China has not yet submitted a protest to Britain regarding the arms embargo. (Reuters Dispatch on the 28th)

The League of Nations Administrative Council Holds a Secret Meeting 214

Discussing the Case of Prohibiting the Supply of Munitions to the Bolivia-Paraguay War

Representative Gu Asks to First Determine Who Is the Aggressor

(Geneva) The League of Nations Administrative Council held a closed-door meeting tonight to consider the British proposal to prohibit the supply of munitions to Paraguay and Bolivia in South America. The Japanese representative did not attend. Gu Weijun represented China at the meeting. After the members of the Administrative Council briefly discussed, they decided to consult with their respective governments. Dr. Gu did not mention the situation in the Far East, but said that it is appropriate to decide who is the aggressor in the war between Paraguay and Bolivia. Hindenburg Issues a New Order to Vigorously Implement Dictatorial Politics 216

Suppressing Freedom of Speech and Assembly

Disturbing Behavior Is Punished by the Death Penalty

Authorities Discover a Major Communist Conspiracy

Martial Law in Berlin, a Large Number of Communists Arrested

Reuters, Berlin, February 28th Hindenburg recently signed a new order. According to the order, Germany will implement an absolute dictatorship and assist it with de facto martial law. The order cancels the articles in the Weimar Constitution that guarantee personal freedom, the right to freely express opinions, freedom of the press, the right to hold meetings and organize societies, the secrecy of letters, telegrams, and telephones, and authorizes the central government to take over the administrative affairs of any state that neglects to restore order. Anyone who attempts to assassinate the president or cabinet members, or commits serious cases such as disrupting public order, rebellion, arson, poisoning, or damaging railways, will be sentenced to death. The order also cancels the articles in the constitution that guarantee the safety of criminals' residences from search, confiscation, and investigation, and orders the authorities of each state to obey the instructions of the central government and implement all orders. The order also stipulates that anyone who commits crimes against public safety or opposes the state must be sentenced to long-term imprisonment or hard labor. Currently, 130 well-known members of the Communist Party and some non-Communist Party members have been taken into custody. The Prussian authorities claimed today that the Communist Party's grand conspiracy to overthrow the current government by force has been discovered and is undoubtedly true. Therefore, they should take the most severe plan to contain the party. When the Berlin Communist Party headquarters was searched, false orders were found addressed to police officers and Nazi stormtroopers, ordering them to put poison in food and drinking water when riots broke out, and to place women and children in front of the "terrorist" groups, and to set fire to various government offices, museums, palaces, factories, and start a regular civil war. According to the authorities, it is now confirmed that the Communist Party has dressed in police and Nazi stormtrooper uniforms and committed acts of rioting in order to attract public hatred. The real leader of this terrorist organization is actually Mu Zengpei, a Communist Party member of the House of Representatives. The police are currently searching for him. The police are now armed and patrolling the areas of Berlin where riots frequently occur by car. All the police in Prussia have been ordered to be on duty day and night to prepare for dispatch until the general election on March 5.

Reuters, Berlin, February 28th Police authorities ordered tonight that all cafes, dance halls, and taverns in Berlin must close at midnight, starting tonight and with no fixed deadline. In peacetime, they must all close at 3 AM, and shopkeepers have been complaining because this measure will cause them significant losses.

Reuters, Berlin, February 28th The site where the Reichstag was burned has been inspected by experts. Today, the members believe that the fire could not have been caused by one person alone. Police authorities also believe that the Dutch Communist Lubai, who was arrested, must have had an assistant, but Lubai has denied it. According to a certain newspaper of the Dutch Communist Party, Lubai was expelled from the party two years ago for committing violence. According to a Reichstag waiter, he saw Lubai talking to two Communist Party members last night, and the two immediately left. One of them was the Communist Party leader Torgler, who turned himself in to the police today and was taken into custody. Many parts of the Reichstag building have been completely destroyed, and it is now believed that it will take at least eight months to repair.

Havas, Berlin, February 28th The losses from the fire in the Federal House of Representatives are not as great as people say. From the outside, it looks as if there has been no fire. Only the furniture and part of the paneling of the inner chamber were destroyed. The central dome is completely intact.

The Siamese Government Promulgates New Elementary School Regulations 218

Siamese Language Actually Accounts for 25 Hours per Week

Overseas Chinese Request a Reduction to Learn Chinese

Reuters, Singapore, March 1 The Siamese government recently promulgated new regulations for Siamese elementary schools, stipulating that each elementary school must teach Siamese for at least 25 hours per week. Because overseas Chinese-run elementary schools have 25 hours per week dedicated to teaching Siamese, there is no time left to teach Chinese. Moreover, Siamese cannot be used outside of Siam, while Chinese is used in all Chinese-populated areas in the East for correspondence and accounting. Therefore, a meeting was held to decide to petition the Siamese government to reduce the Siamese teaching time to 15 hours per week, so that there will be time to learn Chinese.

Roosevelt Appoints Three More Cabinet Members 219

Perkins as Secretary of Labor

This Is the First Time a Woman Has Been Appointed to the Cabinet

Reuters, New York, February 28th President-elect Roosevelt appointed Perkins as Secretary of Labor today. This is the first time that there has been a woman cabinet member in the United States. Ms. Perkins studied sociology at university. In 1912, she was the executive secretary of the New York Public Safety Committee, a position she held for five years. She also served as the executive member of the New York War Relief Organization Committee for one year. From 1926 to 1929, she was the director of the New York State Department of Labor, and since 1929 she has been a member of the New York State Industrial Commission. She has written many books on social economics. Roosevelt also appointed Roper as Secretary of Commerce. Roper is currently a lawyer. In 1917, he served as vice-chairman of the US Tariff Commission, and later served as National Revenue Commissioner for three years. Roosevelt also appointed Senator Walsh as Attorney General. Walsh was once a school teacher, and later studied law. He served as chairman of the Democratic National Convention in both 1924 and 1932.

Japanese Political Turmoil Under Military Domination (Japanese Correspondence) 244

The So-Called Emergency Period Only Causes Social Unrest

The Movement to Overthrow the Cabinet Is Fierce but Controlled by the Military

What the fate of the Japanese Empire will be, even the Satsuma and Choshu clans, which are baring their teeth and claws, annexing Manchuria, attacking Jehol, and firmly contending for the South Seas, cannot figure it out. However, they all feel that the current situation is very dangerous, so they have to adopt a military adventurous policy, hoping to use external military actions as a smokescreen to cover up the ugly situation in their own country. The Tokyo municipal gas bribery case, the riot plans of right-wing groups, the prosperity and growth of left-wing thought... all have an economic downturn as their background, which brewed into the so-called emergency period. Originally, the explanation for the emergency period should be a period of war. Japan neither admits to aggressive invasion nor has formally declared war on our China on the surface, so how can it be said to be an [emergency]? However, if we examine the situation in Japan—especially after the assassination of Prime Minister Tsuyoshi Inukai by active-duty army and navy officers on May 15th last year—the social unrest is indeed reminiscent of wartime. Moreover, there are in fact small-scale wars every day in the three northeastern provinces of China, and large-scale wars are being prepared for in Jehol, eastern Mongolia, and even the Pacific Ocean. The military expenditure for this year has even reached 820 million yen, accounting for 36.5% of the national treasury expenditure of 2.239 billion yen. There is no doubt that it is a quasi-wartime budget expenditure. No one in Japan does not harbor the fear of the descent of the god of war. Although the military advocates various high-sounding arguments and at the same time suppresses speech (in addition to legal restrictions, it also adds the central force of reserve soldiers' associations and other government-controlled groups as forces to coerce public opinion, and casually adds the notoriety of disloyalty to the emperor and unpatriotism, and persecutes them), the awareness of [non-war] is very strong among the people, but it is obscured by the military's war advocacy.

Many people believe that the mission of Saito Makoto's [emergency period] cabinet should be to overcome Japan's current crisis, overcome the anxiety of the general public, and bring the invasion of China to an end. Then it can be said that it has passed through the emergency period and entered a normal state. But everyone understands that the anxiety of Japanese society is unfolding along with the economic panic of capitalism. How can Japan go beyond the scope of capitalism and cast a world of its own? The more the scope of invasion expands, the more difficulties Japan has. The more troops are used, the more difficult the financial problem becomes. The more military spending provokes international dark clouds, the more intense it becomes. For example, with the proposal of the League of Nations' Committee of Nineteen's recommendation, the military's strategy in the diplomatic isolation that Japan has fallen into insists on intensifying the invasion and expanding the scope of the war. From Fengtian to Rehe and eastern Mongolia, let's see what the League of Nations will do. What can the United States do to it? China seems to be even less in its sights, so it only wants to safely occupy Rehe with just over two divisions of troops.

Therefore, the more Saito's cabinet wants to overcome the emergency period, the more serious the emergency period becomes. Social unrest increases, and external wars are even more urgent. However, the political contradictions unfold instead, and the movements to overthrow the cabinet among the factions are still very fierce. First, the military is dissatisfied with the policy. Second, the Seiyukai wants to organize a party cabinet. Third, the Minseitō faction supports Uga Kiyoshi's movement.

The military's policy is indeed dissatisfied with the current cabinet's soft handling. However, Saito is a [nice guy] who does not put forward his own ideas very much, and can let the ministers of each department develop freely. Of course, there is even less of a problem for the army, which looks down on everyone. Moreover, Saito Makoto is also a senior member of the navy, so there has been no active expression of dissatisfaction with him on the part of the army. However, the general public of the Kokumin Domei wants to get close to the political power, so it tries to get close to the army faction and prepares to support Hiranuma Kiichiro, who belongs to the Araki faction, to form a cabinet. But the League of Nations problem has arisen, and it has more political difficulties. I am afraid this is not easy to achieve. Moreover, the fascist cabinet is not supported by financial capital and landlords. As for Yasuda Uchida taking the stage with the military, that is even less likely.

The Seiyukai has an absolute majority of seats, and according to the common sense of parliamentary politics, it should be ordered to form a cabinet, but in the so-called emergency period, the constitution is under the iron heels of the military, so let alone [constitutional convention]. The current cabinet, Saito, has not only not overcome the so-called emergency period, but the war has become even more urgent. The Seiyukai, which is weak and incompetent and hated by the people, must pass through the military, subdue the Minseitō and the Kokumin Domei to control the political power. Moreover, the Tokoji (Takejiro) system and the Kuhara (Fusanosuke) system are mutually opposed (within the Seiyukai itself) and are not under the jurisdiction of President Suzuki, so the possibility of it forming a cabinet must be reduced.

The Minseitō's support for Uga Kiyoshi is a very clever strategy. It can both use it to resist Araki and prevent military dictatorship. Moreover, Uga can also get a lot of sympathy among the military, and has a good impression on the elder statesmen of the upper class. However, the young and vigorous Araki faction will definitely strongly oppose it, especially at a time when they are about to use troops in Rehe, how can Uga intervene? Then, although the Minseito's policy is clever, I am afraid it will not have much practical effect.

Judging from the current political situation, Saito's cabinet is indeed shaking, but it is more suitable than the Suzuki of the Seiyukai and the Hiranuma, who has the tacit agreement of the military. It also has more harmony than Uga, so Saito's cabinet may not fall in the current situation of opposition between factions and diplomatic urgency. However, the possibility of it being reorganized and becoming a [strong] cabinet under the influence of the military is indeed very high, otherwise a purely military cabinet will be established. No matter who comes forward (whether it is Uchida or the others), it does not matter, in fact, it must be completely controlled by the military to be able to cope with the current situation and implement the military's proposed aggressive policy. (February 20th)

International Disadvantage After Japan's Withdrawal from the League of Nations 245

A Tokyo Asahi Shimbun correspondent in Geneva reported that since the failure of conciliation, the temporary general meeting, which included a report of a recommendatory nature as a resolution, has considered Japan's withdrawal from the League to be inevitable. However, the relationship of the entire world to Japan after its withdrawal, according to the opinion of the chief authority of the branch office of our company (Asahi Shimbun) in Geneva, is summarized as follows: (1) The United Kingdom has recently been quite close to China, and is trying its best to contain the actions of the Japanese army, affecting the Tianjin area. However, the United Kingdom is quite suspicious of the United States' attitude. If the United Kingdom obtains the consent of the United States to the report, it can increase the League's assistance in the handling of the Sino-Japanese dispute. Military action in Rehe is very dangerous internationally, but Japan's withdrawal from the League must be realized after giving two years' notice. However, it is questionable whether Japan can fulfill all its international and League obligations (in accordance with Article 1, Paragraph 3 of the Covenant) after withdrawal. From the League's point of view, although Japan is not subject to the General Assembly's report with Article 15 of the Covenant as the limit, Japan should faithfully fulfill the obligation to guarantee territorial integrity and political independence in accordance with Article 10 in its actions in Manchuria. On the one hand, Japan's withdrawal from the League is not desired by the League, but if Japan repents of its withdrawal within two years before the expiration of the term, and returns to the League to succeed to the seat of a permanent member of the council, it is feared that it cannot. Therefore, if Japan rashly withdraws from the League, it will forever lose the right to the seat of a permanent member of the council, and because Japan is listed in the position of a permanent member, it can still interfere in various European problems. If it withdraws from the League, it will lose its world position. As for practical matters, after Japan withdraws from the League, international finance will cut off relations with Japan, and the countries of the League will passively reject Japan. Japan will not be able to raise foreign debt, and Japan will lose all sources of assistance in finance. In addition, the oppression of Japanese goods in various countries around the world has caused serious blows because of the low exchange rate with Japan. Today, various countries are only using tariffs as a strategy to resist Japanese goods. If Japan withdraws and breaks away from its relationship with the League, various countries can avoid the dumping of Japanese goods. At the same time, by quoting Article 16, Paragraph 4, it can remove Japan from the list. If so, Japanese goods will not be able to be dumped freely in the markets of various countries.

It is heard that Tian Songyao, the Sichuan and Shaanxi Bandit Suppression Director, in addition to sending elite troops to suppress the bandits, also decided to completely abandon the interests in Chengdu, concentrating more than 50,000 troops in Bao Ning, Bazhong, Zhao Guang, and other places in northwestern Sichuan to fully suppress them. However, the Red bandits adopted tactics of guerrilla warfare, and used young people as the vanguard, so Tian's suppression has not made progress. Tian felt that his military strength was insufficient, and also due to the lack of pay, he was in a dilemma. At the same time, because of the disagreement between Wei Naixian, commander of the 3rd Division of Tian's forces, and Li Weiruo, commander of the 1st Route, they have been mutually slandering each other since the start of the campaign, and have been hesitant to move forward, resulting in mistakes. Currently, Tian is trying to strengthen the internal unity of the army in order to facilitate the suppression of the bandits. The 24th Army Liu Wenhui, the 28th Army Deng Xihou, and the Sichuan and Shaanxi Army Liu Cunhou have all dispatched troops to assist Tian's army with weapons and pay to launch a general mobilization. It is heard that Liu Xiang and Yang Sen have decided to each send 15 regiments to set off for northern Sichuan. Yang has appointed Xia Jiong as the commander-in-chief of the bandit suppression, and Liu has appointed Guo Xun as the bandit suppression commander, to assist Tian's army as appropriate. Liu Xiang also sent two bombers and two reconnaissance planes to the bandit area to assist, hoping to wipe out the Communist bandits completely in the shortest possible time.

The area of western Hubei was previously occupied by the Red bandits. Chairman Chiang specifically telegraphed the 21st Army Liu Xiang to send troops to assist in the suppression. At the same time, the central government appointed Liu as the commander-in-chief of the bandit suppression in the upper reaches of the Yangtze River, and demarcated 18 counties in western Hubei for Liu to administer. When the Sichuan war broke out, Liu Xiang transferred the bandit suppression troops in western Hubei, totaling more than 18,000 people, completely back to Sichuan to participate in the civil war. The area of western Hubei was then taken over by Xu Yuandong's troops dispatched by Chairman Chiang. Recently, the remnants of the Red bandits He Long, Duan Dechang, etc., have again disturbed the area of Hefeng and Badong, so Chairman Chiang has again ordered Liu Xiang to send troops to take over the defense of the western Hubei area and jointly suppress the bandits. Recently, Liu has assembled troops, preparing to go to Hubei to take over the defense. (February 27th)

Mint Opens Today 247

Opening Ceremony Postponed by Order of the Ministry

Tea and Refreshments Prepared This Afternoon to Entertain Guests from All Walks of Life

The Central Mint was originally scheduled to officially hold its opening ceremony today, and formally start minting at 3:00 PM. The Ministry of Finance also sent Xu Zhan, the director of the Bureau of Currency, as its representative to participate. Yesterday, the factory erected a colorful archway at the entrance of the factory and suspended silk ribbons to decorate it. However, late last night, Director Guo suddenly received a telegram from the Ministry of Finance, stating that in the face of national crisis, everything should be kept simple, and instructing that the opening ceremony be postponed. After receiving the telegram, Director Guo immediately notified this newspaper to inform all walks of life to avoid making a special trip. A reporter inquired with the factory this afternoon, and was told that the opening ceremony has been decided to be postponed, but the formal start of minting will still be carried out at 3:00 PM today, and tea and refreshments will be prepared for guests from all walks of life to visit the contents and work of various departments.

Coinage Situation 248

The reporter first went to the factory this afternoon.

Guided and instructed by Technician Zhang Deqing, they first went to the smelting workshop. The workers were busy with smelting work, putting silver blocks into pots, covering them with coal dust to isolate them from the air and reduce consumption. After the silver blocks were 880 parts per thousand, they were poured into silver bars, which were then rolled into thin sheets using a rolling mill, and then cut short. They were then placed in a blanking machine and stamped into a round shape, and then placed in an oven to heat them for printing. After heating, they were put back into a polishing machine until they were clean and bright. First, the edges were rolled, then the flowers were printed, and the silver dollars were made. Fearing the disadvantage of light and heavy, they were then corrected by a calibrator, and the lighter ones were removed. The silver shavings after smelting were then re-refined in a scrap grinding machine. The factory has a total of 186 workers. The working hours are from 8:00 am to 6:00 pm every day. According to Mr. Zhang, the number of coins manufactured each day has not yet been determined.

Standard Silver Coin 249

The size and thickness of the standard silver coin are the same as the silver dollars currently in circulation on the market, but the two sides are heavier, with a gross weight of 26.691 grams, a fineness of 880, and a pure silver weight of 23.493448 grams. The front is a portrait of the Premier, with the words "Republic of China, Year 21" at the top. The reverse is a sand gull and a sailboat, with the words "One Yuan" on both sides.

Awaiting Orders for Handling 250

The factory has not yet received orders from the ministry, so it has not yet decided whether to allow free coinage or national coinage. Therefore, it has not been possible to contact copper shops or other sectors to commission coinage. Although the new coins have been minted, they cannot be put into circulation because the Legislative Yuan has not yet passed the currency law.

Bandit Suppression Issue 259

Mr. Zhang said that the situation of the Jiang bandits has been quite serious since the end of last year. After the elimination of bandits in northern Hubei, Chairman Jiang and Minister He returned to Beijing, causing the bandit suppression work in Jiangxi Province to be slightly suspended, and the bandits became rampant. Later, Chairman Jiang went to Jiangxi on January 27 at the request of all parties. At that time, he originally planned to return to Wuhan after completing the arrangements, but after inspecting Jiangxi, he felt that it was necessary to suppress the bandits severely, so he decided to divide the army into three routes to suppress them. The eastern route was led by Cai Tingkai, the southern route was led by Yu Hanmou, and the central route was led by Chen Cheng to encircle and suppress the bandits. When Yu arrived in Jiangxi on the 20th, the plan had been completely decided. On the 25th, Yu left Nanchang and had already made contact with the bandit army. Their base covers 13 counties, and their activities cover 45 counties, so it may not be easy to eliminate them in a short time, but after a severe attack, they can be completely eliminated.

Reorganizing Sichuan Politics 260

As for the reorganization of Sichuan politics, we must wait for the Executive Yuan to formulate measures based on the reorganization plan for Sichuan politics in the Republic of China in the 17th year. I have also submitted a suggestion, asking the central government to discuss it. The Central Political Conference was held on the 21st of last month. I did not participate because I went to Nanchang. I don't know the outcome of the discussion. I will definitely wait until there are concrete measures before going to Sichuan.

Hoping That Feng Will Come 263

Mr. Zhang finally told reporters that he would not leave Shanghai for the time being.

Commentary

[The Law of Nature] 269

— Tian Fang

According to a certain evening newspaper yesterday, the New York Times' Beijing telegram said, "[Retired Japanese Imperial Army Lieutenant General] Banzai told a New York Times reporter that the Manchurian people's attitude towards [Manchukuo] is that he believes that [Manchukuo's] self-proclaimed territory can at most only represent a country that once had a national emblem. His opinion is completely different from that of the Japanese military and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, but he firmly believes that Japan will eventually return Manchuria to China. The reason is that [Manchukuo has 30 million people, but they are not truly pure Manchurians,] but [they are all only Chinese,] so [when the Chinese provinces enter a period of peace and order, they will return their individuals and all their land] to China according to the law of nature and necessity." (The above quotations are all from the original text)

China is really fortunate. The land lost by man will actually be returned according to the [law of nature] with [unexpected wonderful effects]. And these words came from the mouth of a [Japanese Imperial Army Lieutenant General], which is even more precious, enough to make the [generals who rely entirely on fate rejoice] and wait quietly for the [final] [return]! Even if they are unlucky enough not to witness it, they can only blame their own short lives and cannot complain that the period is too long.

Finally, what I should be grateful for is that reading this section of the news last night completely dispelled my usual excessive worries and gave me a good night's sleep. Its effectiveness is really no less than [sleeping pills]. I think I can always sleep more soundly from now on—even if I have gentle spring dreams, they will be longer. Here, I cannot but thank this [long-term resident of China], [wearing] [Chinese clothes], [speaking the extremely pure Chinese of Pu Yi's] [close friend], who is not only regarded as a confidant and grateful by the generals who generally advocate the theory of fate!

[Manchukuo's] self-proclaimed territory [now] can at most only represent a country that once had a national emblem." I can swear that I extremely believe this—this is the [law of nature].

Sending Coal in the Snow 270

— Sun Choucheng

An old friend from Gansu, Mr. Deng, sent a letter with a poem in the five-character ancient style, "Sending Coal to Refugees in Hualin Mountain After Snow," which was very tragic. It is transcribed as follows:

Alas, ancient Hugan,

Years of drought and dryness,

How can the people of vegetable color,

Also encounter the chaos of Huamen,

Villages suddenly become ruins,

Wives and children are all scattered,

Travelers cry on the poor road,

Residents dissect their bones,

Fortunately, the great government is virtuous,

Hualin is like a teaching hall,

Thin porridge can continue life,

Better than soberingly灌灌,

Why is the Creator unkind,

The climate suddenly changes,

Flying snow invades the cold bed,

Sharp wind breaks paper curtains,

Alas, I am a man in distress,

Short clothes do not reach the shanks,

Children cry and wail,

How to spend the night,

Dare to fight against hunger and cold,

I am afraid that life and death will be judged,

Moved by this, I cannot sleep,

I sigh three times in the middle of the night,

To seek temporary peace,

First give a lump of charcoal,

And ask philanthropists,

To give generously and make great wishes,

Common Sense of the Protection Method of Steam Boiler Slaves

Since the explosion of the boiler in Zhengtai No. 1 Rubber Factory, which resulted in the death and injury of more than 200 workers, the news has spread, shocking the whole of Shanghai. The local authorities also pay close attention to it because it concerns the safety of the people. The reporter believes that it is too late to dwell on the past, and we can learn from the future. I hope that those who run industrial factories in the future will not be greedy for immediate gains and treat human lives like grass. They should prepare sufficient industrial knowledge to avoid such a major disaster again. It is fortunate among misfortunes. Now, the protection method of steam boilers is described as follows for reference.

The method of protecting boilers is the same as protecting the human body. The first is to keep it clean, so that the minerals contained in the water do not stay in the boiler, so that the surroundings form lumps, reducing the heat transfer power of the iron. Therefore, on the one hand, the water used must be filtered, and on the other hand, the inside of the boiler must be wiped clean once a week. Even the chimney must be cleaned at any time. In addition to cleaning, the second important thing is to pay attention to the number of degrees in the water ting. For example, a furnace that can burn 105 degrees has a cold water pump of 50 pounds, and the water ting burned is only 70 degrees to 90 degrees, which is very appropriate. If it is burned to 120 degrees or 115 degrees, and the pressure valve is also at 120 degrees, then there is a great danger, just like a person who can only carry a load of 100 pounds is asked to carry a weight of 150 pounds, how can he not be overturned? Therefore, we must pay close attention and urge the stoker to check the safety valve at any time.

Other things to pay attention to are the water gauge. If the water in the water gauge is more than an inch high, we open the third valve, and air and water will spray out, which can prove that there is a considerable amount of water in the boiler. If we hold the mouth of the spray with our hands, there is only gas and no water. This is a sign that the water in the boiler is about to run out. At this time, if we do not reduce the heat and pour in a fixed amount of water, the iron plate screws at the bottom of the boiler will first be melted and fall off, and even the boiler will explode.

Sometimes, the small steam pipe leading to the water gauge, the small hole at the end of the pipe, is blocked by dirt in the water, causing the water gauge to lose its effectiveness. Often, no water comes out when the valve is opened, but there is still water in the boiler, or there is water when it is sprayed out, but the boiler has dried up, so we must pay attention.

A boiler can only be used for a maximum of ten years. After a certain period of time, even if the good furnace does not show any pathological conditions on the surface, its material has actually lost its effectiveness. Generally, people who are greedy for immediate gains still cherish such waste and are unwilling to discard it, and eventually repeat the mistake of being greedy for small gains and losing big ones. It is too late to regret it.

In short, workers are greedy and lazy and unwilling to serve wholeheartedly, and industrialists are greedy for profit and have no time to take into account safety issues. As a result, both labor and capital are harmed. Therefore, in order to prevent such disasters, the local government should have the determination—not just a piece of official document to settle the case—to supervise the capital side and not allow them to make do with things. The capital side should have sufficient industrial knowledge to supervise the workers and not allow them to be perfunctory. In this way, industry can have the hope of progress, and human safety can also have a considerable guarantee. I don't know if my proposition can be permitted by the facts and be unimpeded?

Saving the Country Through Aviation 271

— Ying Dai

In China, which is facing a national crisis these days, the most fashionable slogan is no more than saving the country through aviation. There is a lot of talk about airplanes, and you come up with an XX model, and I come up with an XX model. In the near future, China will definitely have a lot more airplanes!

While China is making a big fuss about saving the country through aviation, Japan is also calling for expanding its air force, actively buying airplanes and training aviation talents. Because according to the Japanese themselves, the airplanes that Japan currently has are not enough to defend themselves!

A Japanese person said it well. Zhang Xueliang bought 500 airplanes before the September 18th Incident, but these airplanes were usually placed in warehouses and not used. The main reason was the lack of people, no one to drive them, so when the war broke out, the airplanes in this warehouse were finally given to Japan. If Japan only buys airplanes and does not train aviation personnel, the result will definitely repeat Zhang Xueliang's mistakes.

While everyone is making a fuss about saving the country through aviation, not to mention Shanghai, even Songjiang is shouting about raising donations to buy the Songjiang. Songjiang is a very small place. If Songjiang County buys one Songjiang airplane, then the 60 counties in Jiangsu Province will have at least 60 airplanes. And the whole country may have one or two thousand airplanes. It is not difficult to blow up the entire territory of Japan with so many airplanes, and even if they land, they may occupy the entire territory of the three islands of Fusang!

However, as the Japanese say, if we have airplanes and no one to drive them, the result is just a gift to be given away! We are not opening an airplane exhibition. Even if we exhibit 10,000 airplanes, we will not scare away half an enemy. It can be seen that in the midst of advocating saving the country through aviation, the training of aviation personnel is a matter of urgent importance!

Moreover, flying military airplanes is absolutely different from ordinary airplanes. Just being able to fly is still not enough. At least you must be familiar with the methods of air warfare and the skills of dropping bombs in order to defend the country and defend against the enemy. An aviation person, when facing enemy airplanes in the air, must not be frightened.

Page 20

, even if they are completely surrounded by enemy airplanes, they can only fight bravely. Everything must be practiced and trained daily, otherwise there will be no effect.

Therefore, I hope that the people in various places, while shouting [saving the country through aviation], must also pay attention to the training of the air force.
