Clerk Communication

Even Sages Make Mistakes 272

— Shao Liyu

Editor:

I am a young man with a secondary school education, facing a dead end in terms of family finances and career prospects. Currently, I work as a low-level employee in a semi-Chinese, semi-Western store that sells German goods; it's been a few years now. My daily working hours are from 8:00 AM to 9:00 PM, which is almost thirteen hours every day. Furthermore, I am not allowed to take leave normally; otherwise, my salary will be deducted on a daily basis.

The manager of this store is most fond of those who flatter and fawn, but I have taken a different path and refuse to comply. Therefore, although my work is no less demanding than others, the treatment I receive is not equal. Currently, I only earn a few dollars a month, barely enough for my shoes and socks. Expenses such as travel and medical care are completely out of reach. In addition, he is particularly strict with me in everything. If there is even the slightest mistake, he will fully display the ugly face of a capitalist, saying things like, "There are countless people with your skills in Shanghai, and with rice prices so high, if you make any more mistakes, get out immediately!" I think even sages make mistakes; shouldn't a low-level employee be allowed to make mistakes sometimes? But I dare not speak these words aloud, so I can only swallow my tears. If I were to argue, I would have to pack my bags and prepare to leave.

The calendar on the wall is flying away like snowflakes, and my age is inevitably increasing year by year, and the burden on my family is also increasing day by day. But the oppressor continues to oppress, and the oppressed will never find light. If this continues, what will be the outcome? (To be continued)

Respectfully submitted,

Shao Liyu

Editor's Note: After reading Mr. Shao's letter, we understand that although the store he works in is semi-Chinese and semi-Western, it may not be perfect, but it is much better than completely old-fashioned stores like cigarette paper shops and tea shops. The first paragraph mentions working thirteen hours a day, which is certainly very tiring, but if you think about it, how many stores in Shanghai don't open their doors at 8:00 AM and stay open until late at night? As for their employees, how many of them work in shifts? Thinking about this, I think Mr. Shao might feel more at peace. As for deducting salary for taking leave, I think it's only used to deal with people who take too much leave. Taking twenty days of leave a year would certainly not result in a salary deduction. This is the common practice we know of; Mr. Shao's store should not be an exception.

As for flattering and fawning, it is certainly shameful, and a man of integrity should not do it. At the same time, those who receive flattery and fawning, while they may feel pleased at the time, should also be careful not to consume honey-coated arsenic. We know that if a person has no expectations, who would bow their head and submit to fawn over you? We greatly admire Mr. Shao's ability to stand alone and maintain his integrity. But one thing we believe is that reasonable courtesy towards superiors should not be considered flattery.

"Even sages make mistakes" is a saying worth considering. When a person gains a higher position, they should think this way and forgive their subordinates when they occasionally make mistakes. They should not excessively reprimand them, but use a gentle tone to guide them, hoping that the same unfortunate event will not happen again. However, a person should not use this saying to excuse their own mistakes, because it can make you feel comfortable about your mistakes and not think about improving.

Mr. Shao: We hope you don't compare yourself to those who are better off, but rather compare yourself to those who are worse off. Although you don't need to flatter and fawn over your manager, you must show reasonable courtesy. Strive to be responsible in your work and don't give up on yourself. If you can do this, then you can succeed anywhere; otherwise, other places may not welcome you either!

Fiction

Meishan (Continued) 273

— Written by E.P. Falkowski, Abridged and Translated by Zhixiang (Part 4)

The lights on the main street flowed like the Milky Way in the center of the city. On Saturdays, the workers who toiled for six days in the dark underground felt very happy. Every store was filled with endless hope: "Take me home!" A dress hanging on a mannequin seemed to say.

During this economic downturn, stores eagerly hoped that workers would spend their hard-earned cash on them. Although the alleys were darker than the main street, such jokes were not uncommon, because the alleys were familiar with poverty and could understand it. This silent darkness was illuminated by the ghostly and eerie light of the street lamps. Peter turned into Qilan Street, passed the temporary construction of the Temperance Society, which was originally wasteland, and the great Irish Church. As he walked further, the street gradually became uneven and impoverished, and the plaster on the walls of the houses was largely peeling off. These houses creaked in the cold wind, echoing the sound of mining underground.

At the end of the street, where a round stone pillar stood suddenly like the remains of a huge ancient beast, was the last house. The tilted house displayed a terrifying sight. The sound of a heavily struck piano poured out from the crack in the door. A tattered sign was nailed to the rectangular window: [ ] Butuoer. Peter pushed the door open and walked in. The tavern was filled with noise. Diners sat in a straight line, drinking, smoking, talking loudly, and arguing. John Lewis! The leader of the coal miners' union! His rights and wrongs were the subject of conversation for a group of workers sitting on coal dust in the corner of the room. An old man with bulging veins was retelling the heroic stories of the 1902 strike. Some complained about their meager wages. The old miners were fearful because their work was gradually decreasing. After six days of silent work and sweating in distress, they could now vent freely. But Peter was as silent as he was at home, and found a seat to sit down. John Goodpille—give him a drink. John Goodpille! He was very famous among the coal miners, not only because he was fond of Zhu! He often said that unless he treated his fellow workers well, he would not get anything! But he was a humanitarian. He trusted those workers, gave them wine, and lent them money. He used to be a miner, but now he had savings in the bank, which could be seen from his outward extravagance. His shining head was like a slider. He had a car, and one of his sons was studying at university, hoping to become a lawyer in the future, and another hoped to become a pastor. John Goodpille's life was gradually becoming noble. He could also occupy a position among the successful people in America.

Peter's fingers picked up the glass of wine and felt the aroma of the wine. Around him, many people were arguing fiercely: "John Lewis is a bad guy! Didn't he sell us out in the last contract he signed?"

"Do you think a foreman can have a salary of thousands of dollars a month? There will be an accident soon, right? Do you believe it?"

"Yes!" said a person sitting behind Peter. "Poor Mike Rhodes was crushed to death by a falling rock in the mine today. His wife and three children are really pitiful! He was a good man! Who could have predicted he would have such an encounter! A few days ago, I was still drinking with him!"

"No one can ever predict what will happen today or tomorrow!"

"Peter, old friend, how are you! How is business?" came from the smoke-filled seat on the other side.

Film Special

Tala Birell Narrowly Escapes Assault 274

— Ansen

Difficulties with the American Immigration Authorities

Tala Birell, an Austrian actress with the Universal Film Company in Hollywood, and her sister, Gabriella Birell, are a pair of unique sisters in Hollywood. The two sisters are very affectionate and almost always together, always going out together. The people of Hollywood also care for these two understanding flowers. Unexpectedly, they recently drove out for a tour and accidentally entered Mexico. On their way back, they were harassed by the American immigration authorities and were unable to return or advance, putting them in a very dangerous situation. Therefore, Hollywood's public opinion is unanimously dissatisfied with the immigration bureau's perfunctory handling of affairs. Here is a detailed account:

Tala Birell is fond of traveling. One day, she and her sister Gabriella drove a car south and arrived at San Diego, the southernmost city in California. This place is very close to the Mexican border, and there is a fun place in Mexico called Agua Caliente, where you can swim and gamble, like Monte Carlo in France. Tala suddenly thought of this place, and since it was only seventeen miles away, she couldn't miss it. So the two sisters decided to drive their car to Agua Caliente.

They drove for thirty minutes and arrived at the US-Mexico border. The guards of the US border immigration bureau did not check them, but simply waved their hands and said, "Go ahead." After another hundred steps, that was Mexican territory. The Mexican police also did not cause any trouble, but simply asked the usual question, "Do you have anything to declare?" They answered, "No," and passed safely. They passed through a place called Tijuana and reached their destination. They had breakfast in Agua Caliente, played for half a day, and around 2:00 PM, they took the car and returned along the same route.

On the way, the two of them discussed the beautiful scenery of Agua Caliente and unconsciously returned to the US-Mexico border line. This time, the Mexican police gave them a farewell gift. They waved their hands and they passed. But the US border has always been easy to cross in and difficult to cross out. This time, there were four armed police officers in front of the US immigration bureau who stopped their car. "Hey, what country are you from?" one of the officers asked. Tala replied that they were Austrian.

"Where are your passports?" another shouted loudly.

Coincidentally, Tala had organized all her passports and documents two weeks ago and brought them with her in the car. So she immediately found the passports and handed them to the grim-faced police officer for inspection. They immediately gathered around and carefully examined the passports. Later, one person said, "No, this passport does not have the signature of the American consul in Mexico. You must return to Ensenada and have the American consul sign it before you can come back." "Where is Ensenada?" Tala asked, already panicking.

"Ensenada is on the coast of Mexico, 85 miles from here. If you want to come back today, you must drive fast and return quickly. This place will not allow crossing after 6:00 PM." Tala pleaded with them, saying that these passports were used when they came from Europe and that they did not come from Mexico. They only went to Mexico for fun. But the police officers did not let up at all, so the two sisters had no choice but to retreat into Mexico and go to Ensenada. (To be continued)

Audience Opinions

Impressions After Watching "Orphans of the Sinful Sea" 275

— Qingzhu

Before the system of private property is broken, people in society are constantly disturbed by the issue of inheritance. Some people, because they have inherited the legacy of their ancestors, indulge in taverns and singing halls, developing habits of extravagance and licentiousness, knowing only consumption and not production, creating a class of high-level idlers, which weakens the country and society. Others, because of the unequal distribution of inheritance, cause brothers and sisters within a good family to break down emotionally, fighting among themselves, and going to court to stage all kinds of ugly dramas. We can see these evil phenomena in the newspapers every day. Tianyi Company's "Orphans of the Sinful Sea" aims at depicting the poison of the inheritance system and clearly points out the way out for the wealthy who possess huge assets: they should not harm their descendants with huge inheritances, but should use their wealth to engage in activities that benefit society and establish education for the happiness of the masses. Therefore, the film's intention is so meaningful!

We greatly praise the director's skillful handling of the film. The segmentation of scenes is very appropriate, and the camera angles are also flexible.

Secondly, in terms of actors, especially the child star Shao Suxia, she is indeed a lovely girl. Her lively posture, graceful figure, and acting ability have been well received by the audience in silent films in the past, but this film further demonstrates her acting ability, so her future is promising. Even Ma Loufen's expressions in this film are more advanced than in "Two Orphans in the Battlefield." Hu Shan's villainous role is also passable.

Regarding the scenery: the living room and garden are realistically arranged, and the Tang Dynasty palace is magnificent, tortuous, and exquisite, which can be called a great masterpiece.

Another point is that this film has no subtitles at all, which also opens a new era for domestic films.

Orphans of the Sinful Sea 276

— Ming

From the advertisements in the New Light, we know that Tianyi Company's new sound film "Orphans of the Sinful Sea"—also known as "A Millionaire on the Sea"—premiered yesterday. All those who support domestic films are hoping to know its success, right?

Story

A wealthy man in Shanghai lost his daughter when she was young. He only had a niece left by his deceased younger brother. He planned to adopt her, but she was in love with a young man outside and was living with him. They hired a maid. Coincidentally, the maid's fake father inquired about everything and learned that the maid was the wealthy man's biological daughter. When the wealthy man's brother was alive, in order to seize his brother's property, he stole the daughter and threw her into the river, only to be picked up by him. So he ran to the wealthy man's niece's small house to extort 10,000 yuan, leaving the little maid behind and fleeing to Tianjin. The niece and her lover, knowing that the maid was the wealthy man's flesh and blood, feared that it would be detrimental to them, so they wanted to kill her to silence her. They were forcing her to take poison, but they were reported, and the pair of lovebirds and the "maid's fake father" who fled to Tianjin were arrested and imprisoned.

Director

Mr. Shao Zuiweng did well in general, but he neglected many details. The use of dark writing and phantoms was counterproductive. At the end, the wealthy man's young daughter also entered a civilian school, but she was dressed in fancy clothes, not only had she not shed her class consciousness, but it was also unnecessarily elaborate. However, the interspersed close-ups were extremely satisfying.

Performance

Hu Shanshan is beautiful and elegant, playing a pampered and licentious girl. Her expressions and lines are good, scolding those who worship modern figures, but not as profound as in "Two Orphans in the Battlefield." Ma Loufen is very ordinary. Shao Suxia's performance is small, but her results are excellent. Lu Lixia's great talent is a flash in the pan. Only one segment is interspersed. Zhang Zhenduo is mature and skilled, very good. Wu Yixiao, Qi Zhengmin, and Cang Yinqiu in the supporting roles have amazing achievements and are indeed commendable. Famous actors like Ma Zhengzhong did not appear at all, only a distant shadow flashed by, but his name was listed fourth on the cast list, for some unknown reason. The dialogue and text are very good, but sometimes they seem too few and cannot express the meaning fully, which is open to discussion. The photography is ordinary, and the editing is only competent. The lighting is not very clear. I hope the Tianyi authorities will pay attention to it in the future. It has hindered the photography from being brilliant. The sound is very clear. In some places, it does not match the movements on the screen, which is a pity. The scenery is purely Europeanized, which does not need to be evaluated. The capital has been spent a lot, which is enough to be called great.

Overall

On average, the whole film can be regarded as a work above the water level, because it is a domestic sound film, so it is worth watching.

Mary Pickford's Many Mishaps 277

— Shichun

Not long ago! When Mary Pickford was filming her new film "Secrets," a large lamp suddenly fell, causing a serious shoulder injury. Later, when Mary recovered from her injury and was about to start work, the male lead Wilton Hepburn suddenly resigned, delaying the filming for a few more days. Mary had to find a new male lead and sought the opinions of Cher Ferrell, Luo Lei Cooper, Li Qiudix, Fredrich March, and John McBrown, but to no avail. Finally, she found a famous British actor, Leslie Howard, to play the lead. Just as she was about to start filming, Mary's brother suddenly fell critically ill in Paris, making her distraught and unable to work. Later, her brother called to say that there was a slight improvement, and she continued filming "Secrets." Unexpectedly, after a few days, she received the news of her brother's death, and she stopped working to prepare for her brother's funeral. Mary's "Secrets" has been filmed for the fourth time. The first and second times were abandoned because Mary herself was not satisfied. The third time was delayed due to injury, and the male lead Wilton Hepburn resigned, resulting in it being abandoned halfway. The fourth time it was shelved again because her brother died. It is unknown when the film "Secrets" will be completed. Mary's losses in "Secrets" must be considerable.

"War Comes to Anne" is a masterpiece by Helen Hayes and Gary Cooper, woven into an immortal war love film by the great director Bao Ruoqi of "Seventh Heaven" using scientific techniques.

Various Rumors About Jeanette MacDonald 278

— Shenqi

A few years ago, Hollywood rumored that MacDonald and her fiancé Bob Richey were married, but MacDonald absolutely denied it. Now that MacDonald has gone to Paris, Hollywood is rumored that MacDonald will marry Shiva Lei in Shiva Lei's hometown. However, some people say that MacDonald will marry Bob Richey in Paris and have personally seen Shiva Lei unhappy in Hollywood, which shows that MacDonald will never marry him.

Soviet Film Depicts Turkish War of Independence 279

TASS Moscow, 28th. The Soviet film Toras represents Chai Xi, a famous Soviet playwright. Chai recently returned from visiting Turkey, collecting a lot of materials, and plans to write a film and drama based on the Turkish War of Independence. Chai told Soviet reporters that he stayed in Turkey for six weeks and talked with the famous Turkish writer Nuri, learning about the Turkish War from 1918 to 1922, the current economic situation and life of the Turkish people. He talked with people who participated in the battle and was provided with literary materials by several writers. Chai said, "The new film will depict the Turkish war against imperialism." For those in the Soviet Union, this play is not a chronicle, nor a narrative poem, but a completely psychological drama. The plot is the story of a Turkish youth in the 20th century participating in the battle. Actors from both countries are used, and the explanatory text is also the same. It is also planned to add French explanation. Chai also said that when he traveled to Turkey, he was treated well by the people there. This film will further enhance the friendship between the two countries.

Rereading the Old Story of "Dragon and Tiger Fight" 280

— He

It seems inappropriate to review "Dragon and Tiger Fight" now, but because this film has not been reviewed by various film publications except for one introduction when it premiered in Nanjing, I think it is quite necessary to reread the old story.

Film certainly bears the important mission of art, but at the same time, it also bears a very important responsibility in education. Once we recognize this point, and then review this film, then we can get a more accurate review.

Indeed, this film has no plot and is a disjointed collection of hunting scenes, but it unfolds the great nature of the universe, the survival competition between creatures, and the revelation of beasts killing each other and people benefiting, so it has achieved the mission of film in art and education. It also gives us a kind of hint! A profound hint!

The director of "Dragon and Tiger Fight" can also be said to have achieved considerable success. He can not only skillfully arrange various thrilling battles, but also appropriately insert local customs and many light and humorous fragments. In this case, it can also be said that the director is showing off his cleverness.

In terms of photography, I can assert that it is great and skillful. From various angles, it allows us to clearly see the mutual struggle of various wild animals.

Film Novel

Rasputin (4) 282

— Shi

The Queen had never been so beautiful. She wore a gorgeous palace dress with jewels and stood by the Emperor. She was very proud. Her eyes were sparkling, and her faint smile was easily seen on her slightly parted lips. Seeing her, Paul felt sorrow occupy his heart again. He wished he had the ability to make his master happy all the time! But now, this terrible news was about to come to her. Which of the Russian nobles could be completely sure of what their future held?

The Queen was chatting with Archduke Ferdinand of Austria, her jade-white arms embracing the Crown Prince who stood by her side. The Archduke of Austria represented the Austrian King and presented a gift to the Crown Prince. The little Crown Prince stood solemnly and saluted, asking the Archduke to thank His Majesty the King of Austria. As the Austrian Archduke stepped back, the French Ambassador immediately appeared before them, "Your Majesty! I would like to express the condolences of the Great French Republic for your country's tragic loss. The Archduke was a good friend of our country, and his assassination is deeply lamented by our country."

"Assassinated?" The Queen looked at the Emperor quickly and eagerly. She feared that she, her husband, the one she loved, might be the next one to be assassinated!

"When?" The word jumped out from between the Emperor's firm teeth. He was extremely shocked at this moment, but even in this mood, he did not forget his wife. His hand reached out protectively to touch her.

Paul and looked on, quickly stepping forward. The Queen saw him and said weakly, "Paul, he said Suo Gai...Suo..."

Gai..." Her lips closed in a slight smile. She could not say any more.

"Your Majesty," Paul whispered softly.

"I saw Paul earlier this morning," she said sadly, like a child, "We were watching the new troops of the Imperial Guard...we were still laughing...but now when we see him, we..."

"Your Majesty, I should have reported it earlier," Paul said regretfully. "But I saw how happy you were! I couldn't bear to."

The French Ambassador stepped back. The Queen turned to the Emperor again, "Why did they have to kill him? He loved Russia as much as you do!" She could no longer hold back her tears, which flowed down her fair cheeks. "Now, we only have Paul to be close to."

"Dear!" The Emperor held her hand. "You must be strong...people will see."

"I know..." The Queen sadly restrained herself. People are always watching us! What have we done to make people treat us this way! We..." She cried loudly at this moment. (To be continued)
